=======================|                                |=======================
                       |         Introduction           |             [01.00.00]
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |________________________________|            
{{{

  Thank you for choosing to read my guide on Kingdoms of Amalur: Reckoning. This
guide will strive to provide vital information about the game in a timely and
organized manner. The game is a promising one for a series and a company that is
emerging onto the video game scene.

  This is one of many guides I have written and will complete to the fullest.
Important information, generally quests and unique items, is presented with
[BRACKETS]. There are multiple ways to complete most quests and a wide array of
play styles, I will do my best to accommodate to all styles in the guide.

}}}

=======================|                                |=======================
                       |           Controls             |             [02.00.00]
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |________________________________|            
{{{


 PC
¯¯¯¯
Left Mouse  - Attack
Right Mouse - Use Equipped Spell
W           - Up
A           - Left
S           - Down
D           - Right
L Shift     - Block
Space       - Dodge
L Control   - Sprint
C           - Stealth Toggle
Numbers 1-0 - Equip Spells
F           - Interact
Q           - Use Alternate Weapon
X           - Enter Reckoning Mode
E           - Quick Mana Potion
R           - Quick Healthy Potion
H           - Toggle Aggressive Mode
Tab         - Usable Items
Esc         - Pause
M           - Map
I           - Inventory
P           - Abilities Page
O           - Skills Page
L           - Quest Log

 XBOX 360
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
X             - Primary Weapon
Y             - Secondary Weapon, Toggle Map (World/Local)
B             - Dodge
A             - Sprint, Action (Talk, Harvest)
Start         - Menu
Black         - Map
Right Trigger - Display Skill Menu
Right Button  - Stealth Mode
Left Trigger  - Block
Left Button   - Potion Menu
D-Pad &lt;-      - Health Potion
D-Pad -&gt;      - Mana Potion
D-Pad ^       - Hostile Mode (While in Towns)

 PS3
¯¯¯¯¯
Square   - Primary Weapon
Triangle - Secondary Weapon, Toggle Map (World/Local)
Circle   - Dodge
Cross    - Sprint, Action (Talk, Harvest)
Start    - Menu
Select   - Map
R1       - Display Skill Menu
R2       - Stealth Mode
L1       - Block
L2       - Potion Menu
D-Pad -&gt; - Health Potion

}}}

=======================|                                |=======================
                       |          Characters            |             [03.00.00]
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |________________________________|            
                        ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{

 ALYN SHIR
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Diplomat, spy, or saboteur, few things are certain about the secretive
Dokkalfar agent named Alyn Shir. Most know her as a charming and scandalous
ambassador. The Alfar armies know her as a cunning and unpredictable ally. A
rare few know her as a fearsome and merciless assassin—but never for long. When
asked, Alyn Shir is willing to spin any number of tales about her past.
Sometimes, she is the least daughter of a minor noble, inheriting only a pair of
ancient daggers and a disdain for those who think that power will protect them.
In others, she was born a street urchin and survived through stealth and
cunning. The only certainty is that as the war rages on, this singular woman has
found more and more need for her knives, and no one can be certain where her
true loyalty lies.

 AGARTH, FATEWEAVER
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Once known across Amalur as the Blade of Avgruun, Agarth was renowned for his
exceptional courage and strength. With each victory, word of his combat prowess
spread throughout the Faelands. Agarth had wealth, power, and prestige. But more
than a decade ago, Agarth retired his blade, shocking those who knew him best.
Offering little explanation, he gave away the riches he had earned and joined
the Fateweaver order.

  Agarth had discovered that he possessed the gift of foresight. Unfortunately,
his insight into Fate brought him troubling visions. He turned to the bottle for
refuge, falling from his former glory into obscurity and anonymity. Although
Agarth now hides behind the haze of drink, those who look close will see a man
whose greatness can still return...

 HIGH KING TITARION
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  The High King of the Summer Court has ruled his people with the warmth and
ageless vision of the ancient sun. Unlike most Fae, who look on mortals with
caution, Titarion is eager to share his wisdom with the young races. Beloved by
all in the Court of Summer, he sits above the politics of the court. However,
with Gadflow's treachery and the breaking of the Great Cycle of the Fae,
Titarion’s radiance has fallen into shadow.

  Now the Summer King broods upon his throne, troubled by the changes that
herald the end of his kingdom. His subjects fear for him, for the Fae have never
known change or true death, and they cannot understand his warnings. For now,
Titarion must wait, hoping for a way to prevent the Long Winter.

 TEMPLAR OCTIENNE
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  With a personal fortune and authority over dozens of the greatest gnome
Scholars of the age, Templar Ligotti Octienne wields power and influence other
gnomes can only aspire to. However, his own aspirations reach much further than
mere wealth or victory in the political games of Adessa’s council.

  Octienne is known among the other Templars for his arrogance. Some even dare
whisper that a number of the projects he supports defy the laws of Adessa,
although no proof of misdeed has ever been presented to the other Templars.

  Octienne is a gifted scholar in his own right, but he left the academy for
political pursuits, believing his goals were better served in the Forum. He has
used his influence among the Templars to support the development of the Well of
Souls and few know of the project’s true goal. Despite the difficulty of
protecting the Scholars in his employ from the scrutiny of the outside world
and the dangers of the war-torn countryside, Octienne is confident he will
succeed in his plans.

 GENERAL TILERA
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  When the Tuatha marched on the Plains of Erathell without warning 12 years
ago, the Alfar hastily organized an army under the command of General Tilera at
Gwydion to strike back against the assault. Although the campaign was costly,
Tilera eventually drove the enemy out of Erathell and back into the swamps of
Klurikon.

  But the war was not over. Tilera’s loss following the appearance of the
monstrous Balor on the Day of the Pale Swans allowed the Tuatha to push back and
lay siege to the fortress of Mel Senshir. And there the battle lines of war have
stood for the past nine years.

  Tilera, ashamed of her failure even in the face of such hopeless odds,
resigned her commission and set out on a journey to uncover an ancient weapon
that legends say can kill the Balor. Tilera knows that it is only a matter of
time before the Tuatha call the Balor to the walls of Mel Senshir, turn the tide
of the battle in their favor, and sweep across the Faelands once again.

 FOMOROUS HUGUES
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Focused, dedicated, and visionary -- these words have all been uttered in the
great Librarium of Adessa about the Scholar Fomorous Hugues. Little is known
about Hugues’ life before his graduation from the academy. Following a brief
professorship in Adessa, Hugues dedicated himself to a single project: the Well
of Souls. The benevolent professor seeks to cease all war and, indeed, prevent
any sentient mortal creature from meeting an unnatural end.

  Although the project has yet to yield a success, the Fateweaver Agarth has
seen it written in Fate’s tapestry that Hugues will succeed. Unfortunately,
Agarth has also foreseen that Hugues’ success will come at the cost of his own
life.

}}}

{{{
  The races in the vast world of Amalur have varying racial traits and worship
different Patron Gods. Choose wisely when creating your character as it will
effect, though minimally in the long run, your play through.
 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                              L j o s a l f a r                               |
|                                                                              |
|  A proud and insular people, the Ljosalfar strive to preserve nature and     |
| shape it to their will. The light elves resist change, flash-freezing their  |
| ancient homeland to keep it in an idealized, timeless state. The Ljosalfar   |
| revere the principle of Justice, fighting time and again to defend Amalur    |
| against chaos and darkness.                                                  |
|                                                                              |
|  The light elves stand with their Dokkalfar cousins to battle the relentless |
| armies of the Tuatha. Though far from their frozen homeland, the Ljosalfar   |
| are determined to keep the fortress of Mel Senshir from falling into the     |
| hands of their enemy.                                                        |

|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                                 V a r a n i                                  |
|                                                                              |
|  The human clans known as the Varani can be found throughout Amalur, as much |
| at home on the high seas as in the villages and outposts they inhabit.       |
| Though not as culturally refined as the Almain, the Varani have brought      |
| commerce and a degree of civilization to the wilds of the Faelands.          |
|                                                                              |
|  While lacking political motivation for involvement in the war against the   |
| Tuatha, many Varani have found employment fighting in the mortal armies as   |
| mercenaries. The battle-hardened fierceness of the Varani has given them a   |
| well-earned reputation as a valuable ally in the seemingly unwinnable        |
| conflict.                                                                    |

 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                              D o k k a l f a r                               |
|                                                                              |
|  The Dokkalfar are respected as sophisticated students of magic and          |
| diplomacy, yet it is their alluring presence that makes them so compelling.  |
| The dark elves are the ultimate manipulators, controlling the actions of     |
| others from the shadows. While their reputation for subtlety is well earned, |
| many find the Dokkalfar so charismatic that they willingly parlay with them  |
| -- regardless of the consequences.                                           |
|                                                                              |
|  Though the port city of Rathir stands as a testament to their thriving      |
| culture, the relentless war against the Tuatha has put a great strain upon   |
| the Dokkalfar. The dark elves fight alongside their fairer-haired cousins,   |
| the Ljosalfar, in an attempt to push back the unyielding armies of the Fae.  |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|

|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                                 A l m a i n                                  |
|                                                                              |
|  The Almain are valorous humans who embody the ideal of Order in all things. |
| They abhor Chaos, imposing structure and ritual in everything they do. One   |
| of the most imperialistic kingdoms in Amalur, the Almain are proud of their  |
| long and illustrious military tradition. Their patron deity is Mitharu, god  |
| of Order, a belief that guides every aspect of their lives.                  |
|                                                                              |
|  Some Almain have come to the Faelands seeking freedom from the binding ties |
| of politics and religion, hoping to make their own destiny far from the      |
| rigid laws of their kingdom. Yet no matter how far they may wander from      |
| their homeland, they honor the battlefield disciplines of their ancestors.   |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|

PATRON GODS
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  These deities are worshipped by those who live in Amalur and grant blessings
to their loyal worshippers. Each race only follows five Gods and these small
bonuses can add up to turn the tide in battle, so be careful what you choose.
 ____________________________________________________

=======================|                                |=======================
                       |           Destinies            |             [05.00.00]
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |________________________________|            
                        ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  Mortal creatures in Amalur believe they are born with their destinies already
woven into Fate’s grand tapestry. But when Reckoning's Fateless Hero dies and is
reborn outside the weave, the path ahead is left mysteriously open. By unlocking
and exploring Destinies, you'll plan your own path to victory, outside the
bounds of fate.

  Destinies allow you to develop and master your personal battle style, crafting
your character without the constraints of traditional classes. With Destinies, a
battle-hardened warrior can incorporate the stealthy quickness of a rogue and
the magical mastery of a sorcerer, or adopt subtle variations of them all.
Destinies can grant new powers, bonuses and combat options to help you on your
journey through Amalur.

  Some of your choices will so profoundly affect life's fabric that your destiny
will be permanently altered through Twists of Fate, unique player bonuses
granted at key moments in your adventure. Your Destiny is formed as you place
points into Might, Finesse, and Sorcery. Bonuses are associated with the Destiny
you have molded, enhancing damage and skills to suit your play style. The more
points you put into the abilities the higher you advance through the tiers.
 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                                   M a g e                                    |
|                                                                              |

|               +13% Magic Damage      | to the shadows, wielding the arcane,  |
|               1/2 Equip Requirements | or trading blows in a melee. Because  |
|               +1 to all Skills       | you are used to life on the road, you |
|               +5% Damage Resistance  | are tougher than the average denizen  |
|                                      | of Amalur.                            |
|==============================================================================|
|                                   PRODIGY                                    |
|==============================================================================|
| Requirements: 17 in all Abilities    |  The various interest and pursuits of |
| Bonuses:      +15% Melee Damage      | the Prodigy include all types of      |
|               +15% Ranged Damage     | weapons, magic, and armor. You are    |
|               +15% Magic Damage      | acclimated to a rugged lifestyle and  |
|               1/2 Equip Requirements | naturally resistant to all attacks.   |
|               +1 to all Skills       | You also have a greater chance to     |
|               +7% Damage Resistance  | land a critical strike.               |
|               +5% Chance to Crit.    |                                       |
|==============================================================================|
|                                  POLYMATH                                    |
|==============================================================================|
| Requirements: 26 in all Abilities    |  Your experience with the varied      |
| Bonuses:      +17% Melee Damage      | dangers of Amalur has honed you into  |
|               +17% Ranged Damage     | a dilettante of combat. Felling       |
|               +17% Magic Damage      | countless foes has prepared you for   |
|               1/2 Equip Requirements | any battle.                           |
|               +2 to all Skills       |                                       |

|               +7% Chance to Crit.    |                                       |

|               +20% Magic Damage      | legend of prowess finesse, might, and |
|               1/2 Equip Requirements | sorcery. Few are your equal in one of |
|               +3 to all Skills       | these specialties, and there are none |

 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

                       |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |          Walkthrough           |             [06.00.00]
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |________________________________|            
                        ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  After the opening scene and you have regained control, you are awakened in
the Well of Souls.

 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|                             Out of the Darkness                   [06.01.00] |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ITEMS:      Cloudy Protection Shard  [ ]  Disposal Notes                 [ ] |
|             Minor Healing Potion     [ ]  Spider Memo                    [ ] |
|             Well Progress Log        [ ]                                     |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| EQUIPMENT:  Squire's Ring            [ ]                                     |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ENEMIES:    Giant Rat                     Giant Spider                       |
|             Rock Troll*                   Tuatha Soldier                     |
|______________________________________________________________________________|
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  Move across the narrow bridge and into a new section. On the right side you
can toss the remains into the fire but straight ahead is a door where a
skeleton holds a [RUSTY SWORD]. The door will open but disregard for now and
move to your left to find an [DISPOSAL NOTES] on the table and a [SKELETON]
further along. Make your way through the door where you can hear screams and a
man. Disregard them for now and follow the path into your first battle against
some Giant Rats.

  With the vermin defeated, continue down the hallway and rescue the gnome
under attack. Jump down from the platform and fight off the Tuatha Soldiers. Be
sure to loot their corpses and the [CHEST] nearby. Ask Encel any questions you
might have, accept his [MINOR HEALING POTION x3], and proceed through the large
door he opens.

N o t e
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Barrels, crates, and other wooden objects are easily broken when you attack
them. Be sure to destroy these objects everywhere you go as they hold numerous
items, but more often than not gold.
_______________________________________________________________________________

  Another short scene occurs when you reach the top of the stairway. Move across
the water to the portcullis which can be raised with the nearby lever. Break the
crates to the right as you enter the next room to find a [CHEST]. To the north
another [CHEST] hides behind crates and the [SHIELD] you were looking for is on
the nearby weapons rack. Equip the Shield and a hole is blown into the wall as
more Tuatha Soldiers attack. Defeat them and loot the [BOW] then equip it into
your secondary slot.

  Ahead are some archers, so switch to that brand new bow and pick them off.
Encel will open the next door into an area with a [CHEST] hiding behind some
crates. Kill the Tuatha Soldiers on the second level and pick up the [DAGGERS]
as you move into an area with a waterfall. To your left is a [CHEST] behind some
crates, loot it and proceed up the ramp where you must perform a stealth kill.
Slay the other Tuatha Soldiers that are just picking off the helpless then move
into the next room.

  Use your magic when told then begin looting the area. On the table to the west
is a [SPIDER MEMO] and just south of that a [CHEST]. Proceed through the
corridor and into the cave-like area. At the fork stay straight to find a
[CHEST] then double back west to find a Giant Spider. Loot the corpse for a
[STAFF] then equip it so you can burn the spider webs. Defeat the three Giant
Spiders and loot the [SPIDER SAC] before continuing south through another web.
Slay two more Giant Spiders and open the [CHEST] as you make your way into the
armory. A scene occurs and if you pass the Persuasion Check with Encel you can
receive additional [POTIONS]. Loot the three [CHESTS] and make your exit.

  Up the stairway you find the Well of Souls. Move along the left side to find
the [WELL PROGRESS LOG] then enter the Laboratory. Speak with Fomorous Hugues
and ask any questions you might have. When you are ready to go, a scene takes
over and you must escape. At the top of the steps are two Tuatha Soldiers and
to the north side of the room a [CHEST]. Proceed through the doorway and
continue your ascent, but don't pass the [CORPSE]. This next door opens up to
the first boss, the Rock Troll.

 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                                 Rock Troll                                   |
|                                                                              |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|  The Rock Troll has two attacks, a lunging forward swing used at melee and   |
| a slam that sends energy in a line towards you, often used at range. The     |
| melee attack has to be blocked or dodged, simply running to avoid the attack |
| doesn't work since the Troll can pivot quickly and still reach you. The      |
| ranged attack is easily sidestepped and can be dodged at a forward angle to  |
| quickly close the distance for melee strikes. Overall, this fight isn't that |
| difficult as long as you dodge and then counter with combinations.           |
|                                                                              |
| Drops: Squire's Ring, Cloudy Protection Shard, 35 Gold                       |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  With the Rock Troll defeated, exit to Allestar Glade to complete the opening
quest.

}}}
 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|                               Into the Light                      [06.02.00] |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ITEMS:      Anonymous Journal        [ ]  Codex of Destiny               [ ] |
|             Health Regen Potion      [ ]  Mana Regen Potion              [ ] |
|             Rikka's Journal          [ ]  Stonecandle Log                [ ] |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| EQUIPMENT:  DLC/Pre-Order Armor (Set)[ ]                                     |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ENEMIES:    Bear                          Boggart                            |
|             Brownie                       Ettin Brute                        |
|             Ettin Shaman                  Ettin Warpriest                    |
|             Giant Rat                     Giant Spider                       |
|             Kobold                        Kobold Rogue                       |
|             Kobold Savage                 Red Legion Archer                  |
|             Red Legion Bandit             Sprite                             |
|             Tuatha Raider                                                    |
|______________________________________________________________________________|
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  You most likely have gained a level, so be sure to set your skills and the
ability points. Jump off the platform nearby into the water and use the [DIVE
POINT] to find a few items. To the east you can swim behind the waterfall to
find four Giant Rats guarding quite a bit of treasure. Back in the water you
can find a second [DIVE POINT] to the far west on the opposite end. Back on the
land you can talk with the various gnomes and loot the [OVERTURNED CART].

N o t e
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Across the land you will find various flowers and herbs that can be harvested
for their reagents. They glow and have sparkles coming out of them so they are
somewhat difficult to miss. Be sure to stop at them and acquire the reagents
along your journey.
_______________________________________________________________________________


  Near the cart you can find a [SHRINE OF MITHARU] that will provide a bonus.
You can hear a gnome ask for assistance with a Bear, so provide the help via
slaughter. You can talk with Guran and perform a Persuasion Check to receive
about [100 GOLD]. As you progress south you can notice a few Wolves near a cart.
Slay them and move down this narrow path to gain access to a new area, the
Stonecandle Mines. Enter the mines and take the eastern path to find [CHEST],
but beware the bear trap in front of it. The western path leads to a few
Kobold Rogues, be careful.

  Further along is another Kobold and if you continue to move northeast you
will complete a circle. There are Kobold Rogues along the way and they aren't
the easiest of enemies to kill. Near the far east of the circular path is a
Gnome with the [STONECANDLE LOG] on his corpse. The southern part of the fork
leads to a locked [CHEST]. Leave the cave and take the other path to start a
scene with Agarth the Fateweaver. Mid-conversation you can perform a Persuasion
Check to receive [GREATER HEALTH REGEN POTION] and a [GREATER MANA REGEN
POTION].

  Tuatha Soldiers and Rogues appear and you learn how to use Reckoning. After
some more conversation you get a chance to choose your Destiny. A new objective
is added and you regain control. Loot the [SACK] then proceed east where you
will pick up the quest [SPECIAL DELIVERY]. Ahead is a [DALENTARTH STONE] that
will give you a few experience and some lore. Further ahead you will enter the
town of Gorhart. Speak with Herc Adwold to start the quest [BUILDING BRIDGES]
and speak with Father Dynwel to start [CRISIS OF FAITH].

Special Delivery
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  You can find the [CHEST] near the Inn that gives any DLC or Pre-Order gear
you might have unlocked.
_______________________________________________________________________________

  Enter the Corner Shop and sell all your excess wares then loot the
[BLACKSMITHING SUPPLIES] in the back room. You can use the Blacksmith Forge to
the right of this chest if you need to craft new weapons/armor. Head upstairs
and you can steal [RIKKA'S JOURNAL] from the dresser. Enter the Alchemy store
and speak with Nanne Hanri to start the quest [RECIPE FOR TROUBLE]. In the
basement you can unlock a [CHEST] and steal from the [BOOKSHELF] to obtain the
book [CRIPPLESPORE CAPS]. At this time you can proceed along the road and reach
the destination for the main quest or start some of the various quests that this
town has to offer.

To the Fateweaver
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Continue east along the road until you come across Ainmhi. You can start the
quest [RED IN TOOTH AND CLAW] if you decide to help him. Further along the road
you will find Penri Kell who can offer the task [REPRISAL, REPRISED]. Move south
from here and slay the beasts that attack you. Along the road you eventually
come across Arden's Hut. After the scene leave the area and move south to the
village of Canneroc. West from here along the road you can spot the remains of
a Silkfarmer from Canneroc, looting it starts the task [RESTING THE BONES].

  Make your way around the bend and you will be ambushed by a large group of
Giant Spiders and Venomspitters. As you approach Hornstead you can find an
[ETTINEMERE STONE]. Stick to the road in this area, the enemies are plentiful
and powerful. As you make your way to the objective you can loot a corpse to
start [RALLYING CRY]. Help Agarth slay the Shaman then enter Dellach.

The Theatre of Fate
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Move through the hallway into an open room with Wolves and an Ettin Brute.
You will find much of the same in the next room as well as a Dispel Ward
[CHEST]. Follow the path and open the magnificent door to find Kobolds that have
gathered. Loot the nearby [CHEST] and continue down the hallway to find a single
Kobold. Approaching it summons a horde of Kobold Rogues, so be alert and fight
them one at a time. Open the elegant door and continue along the path to another
room filled with Kobold. There is a [CHEST] in the corner on your way out of the
room into another where Kobolds are battling the Ettin.

  Further in you will fight an Ettin Warpriest. Treat the fight like the Rock
Troll and it will be a cakewalk. Attempting to hack and slash combo this foe
isn't going to work at your level. After the short scene proceed west through
the empty room but check the north and south rooms to find [CHESTS]. Continue
into a hallway with Kobold Rogues then south through a corridor and clear out
the last Kobolds as you enter the Theatre of Fate.

  The Niskaru Bloodhunters that you face are easily beaten if countered after
blocking. It becomes easy to chain combo them and with Agarth there to aid you
they go down even quicker. Loot the [CHEST] for the [BAND OF THE DUELIST] then
touch the Destiny Stone to receive the [CODEX OF DESTINY]. A short scene occurs
and you are thrown into combat. Use large area attacks to quickly fell the would
be assassins. A short scene occurs and this quest completes.

}}}
 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|                            Old Friends, New Foes                  [06.03.00] |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ITEMS:      None                                                             |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| EQUIPMENT:  Nyralim's Sidhe          [ ]                                     |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ENEMIES:    Barghest                      Boggart Tumbler                    |
|             Brownie                       Faer Gorta                         |
|             Gnarsh*                       Murghan                            |
|             Rock Troll                    Sprite                             |
|             Sprite Frost Champion         Tuatha Raider                      |
|______________________________________________________________________________|
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  Leave the area and loot the [CHEST] on the left before jumping down. Slay the
two Ettin Brutes and open another [CHEST] to before leaving this section. Make
your way up north past Gorguath and into the House of Ballads, you should pass
by an [ODARATH STONE] along the road as well as a locked [CHEST]. Enter the
House of Accolades and speak to Alyn Shir. Give the Codex to Glianal who
dismisses the Codex and calls is a fake. Alyn wants you to seek out the King,
but it's quite a journey. Prepare yourself for the trek and get moving to the
southeast.

  Past Canneroc you can continue east and fight off the Murghan across a bridge
where a locked [CHEST] resides. Go passed the library and over another bridge
where more Murghan lurk. You can spot Declan Malus just off the path to start
the quest [A BRUTAL CONTRACT]. Try to avoid the Mountain Trolls at this time
and continue up passed Grim Onwig will start the quest [THE GUIDED HANDS]. Move
east until you reach Vorm Lodge. This is usually a good place to make a pit stop
before heading south to your goal; you can start the side quests [AGGRESSIVE
BROWNIES] and [DANGERS OF THE SIDHE].

  Leave the inn and head south, slaying the enemies in the way until you reach
Caer Nyralim. Follow the path all the way to the top and speak with Nyralim.
With some words of wisdom and guidance, you are sent to defeat the Troll
Matriarch Gnarsh. The fastest way there is to warp to the Ballads Library and
head south. Kill the Rock Troll guarding the entrance then enter Haxhi Dam. Here
you meet up with Alyn Shir once again and she will assist you throughout this
dungeon.

  To the north another Rock Troll attacks. You should have these down pat by now
so quickly dispatch and continue north. The Tuatha seem to have made it here as
well, so kill them and move around the bend. South of here is a group of Tuatha
Raiders just sitting around. You can sneak up on them with Alyn or just charge
in full force. Move east across the bridge where a Rock Troll and two more
Tuatha Raiders are working. Kill them and continue east where four Tuatha have
their backs turned to you. As you begin to fight them a Rock Troll will burst
through the wall so be on guard.

  Further along are more Tuatha Raiders and another Rock Troll. You can craft
gems at the Sagecraft Altar and loot the two [CHESTS] in the northern alcove.
Continue east where you can find three [CHESTS] in a small alcove to the south.
Head up the stairs to find the Troll Matriarch, Gnarsh.

 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                                   Gnarsh                                     |
|                                                                              |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|  Gnarsh has significantly more health than a normal Rock Troll but she       |
| functions all the same. The key difference is that her lunge is faster and   |
| follows up her overhead smash with a side swipe so you can't roll to one     |
| side and just start cutting into her. Roll back and counter with a Storm     |
| Bolt which has a chance to stun the Troll. This should allow for some combos |
| to whittle down her massive health.                                          |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Speak with Alyn Shir after you've slain the beast. Fast Travel back to Nyralim
and report the good news. Pass the Persuasion Check and you can obtain
[NYRALIM'S GRACE]. With more words of wisdom, head to Sidhe and slay the Sprites
that appear along the road. As you move through the water you can find a [STONE
OF SIDHE]. Cross the bridges and enter The Gardens of Ysa to meet Chancellor
Erawn who completes this quest.

}}}
 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|                             The Hunters Hunted                    [06.04.00] |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ITEMS:      None                                                             |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| EQUIPMENT:  Random Ring              [ ]                                     |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ENEMIES:    Tuatha Archer                 Tuatha Raider                      |
|______________________________________________________________________________|
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  Enter the Three Lamps Inn at Didenhil and talk to Agarth. You will receive a
random ring and then be on your way to the Hunter's Pit.

Hunter's Pit - West (Main Gate)
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  If you chose to take the front gate then expect quite a few enemies. The first
camp is littered with foes, a use of Reckoning here is a decent choice. Loot the
[CHEST] on the west end then continue north. As you turn the corner you will
encounter more Tuatha and another [CHEST] in the northern camp. Continue east
and break the crates along the bridge to call two more Tuatha Raiders. There is
a Hidden Door to the south but it's only useful if your Detect Hidden is high
enough to see; there are three [CHESTS] behind the door.

  Further east you will find a long Tuatha Raider. Jump down into the next camp
where a large group will attack you from range. Fight fire with fire and pick
the Raiders off from distance. Break the crates to discover a hidden [CHEST]
then move up the ramp as you march east. Slay another group of Tuatha and you
will enter the main room with Agarth meeting up with you. Gadflow will be
summoned and a short scene occurs. Agarth suggests you take up the offer Alyn
Shir had earlier. Loot the [CHEST] and search the other half of the Pit before
leaving.

Hunter's Pit - East (Back Door)
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Enter the back gate and kill the Tuatha Raider. You can sneak past the camp if
you want just watch out for the bear trap. Ahead is a floor trap and arrow
launcher, then another bear trap. Past the waterfall is another bear trap and a
group of Tuatha near a [CHEST]. Past here you can release the Barghests that
won't attack you but instead attack the Tuatha further along. Grab the [CHEST]
and go south to find another one. Return back to the north and pick the lock on
the door.

  Head into this room and start slaying all the Tuatha. Break the crystal and
Gadflow comes out for a chit-chat. Don't miss the [CHEST] and search the other
half of the Pit before leaving.

}}}

|                              The Coming Storm                     [06.05.00] |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ITEMS:      Twist of Fate - Unwritten One [ ]                                |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| EQUIPMENT:  None                                                             |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ENEMIES:    None                                                             |
|______________________________________________________________________________|
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  With both quests completed you can now visit the High King. In the Gardens of
Ysa head east into the Font then into the Court of Summer. Place the Codex of
Destiny and a scene occurs. At the end of the scene you receive the [TWIST OF
FATE - UNWRITTEN ONE]. The quest ends and you once again must speak with Agarth
and Alyn Shir. Once you have done so, pick your destination.

{{{
  Make your way into Detyre by following the road east. Once there you can
encounter a woman named Frama Aedic who starts the side quest [KIDNAPPED]. Keep
to the road or short-cut through the dangerous wild as you make your way across
Alserund and into the Hollowlands. The joint path has several Boggarts but
nothing of concern. Stop by Eagonn's Tomb for a travel location then go south
past the Motus Mining Outpost and button hook around to reach Templar Octienne
at the Overlook Camp. Head south in search of Fomorous Hugues and into the
Saltwell Caverns.

  Kill the Faer Gorta in the entrance and smash some crates to find two [CHESTS]
and on one of the tables [SALTWELL LAB NOTES, DAY 21]. Loot the [LAB KEY] from
the Gnome Corpse in the next room. Several Sons of Laz, slow moving Zombie-like
creatures, appear to kill you. Use the key to open the next door where more
Sons of Laz appear. Kill them and open the [CHEST], grab [SALTWELL SITE LAB
NOTES, DAY 142] and loot the Gnome Corpse for the [EMERGENCY SUPPLY KEY]. You
can use this key to open one of the [CHESTS] in the first room if you couldn't
unlock it or save it for one that's ahead.

  Be careful of the tripwire on the way into the corridor, as well as the arrow
launcher trap. Kill the Faer Gorta Sentinels that attack in the next room and
snag [SALTWELL SITE LAB NOTES, DAY 233] off the northern table. As you continue
east there is an incinerator at the southern end. Wake the Sons of Laz and use
the lever to incinerate them for easy experience. There is also a [CHEST] in
this area but beware the Spike Traps. The next room has several Sons of Laz and
as you fight them off several more spawn from the direction you came. Loot the
Gnome Corpse for another [EMERGENCY SUPPLY KEY] then open the door south.

  To the east are a few Faer Gorta and two [CHESTS]. Continue south to start a
short scene with Hugues then defend him from the White Palm. Speak with Hugues
then loot the two [CHESTS] and be on your way.

|                           Enemies in High Places                  [06.07.00] |

{{{
  Set your compass east and get moving, you have to cross through two entire
zones just to get to the Templar Jorielle. As you cross into Menetyre you can
find a Hidden Door that leads to a few new objects. You will also pass two
[STONES OF THE HOLLOWLANDS] and a [STONE OF SPRING]. Take a straight shot across
this zone and at the juncture to Apotyre you will find the first [APOTYRE STONE]
Continue east until you approach the Darkvari Outlaws, one of which drops the
[MOTUS MINING DOCUMENTS]. Reading this note starts the task [WHITESTONE
TARNISHED].

  Continue your journey to Adessa where you can spot a [STONE OF SUMMER]. You
are stopped and questioned as you enter the city and then given the [VILLA KEY]
to enter your new home. Venture south and enter the Domus Politica and go up
the stairs to find Templar Jorielle. She isn't buying what you're selling but
tells you of a way to prove your point. As you exit you are stopped and given
the location and direction of your task. Seek out Octienne in the Livrarium and
chase after him as he escapes.

|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |

|  The most important thing to remember is that you cannot kill Octienne until |
| he has reached the final point of the chase. With this in mind, focus on the |
| Whitepalms that he continually unveils as you chase him, they must be        |
| defeated in order for Octienne to continue running. Dodging will be your     |
| best friend as Octienne shoots Fire and Ice balls that can bombard you       |
| repeatedly, leaving you open to the minions. Reckoning is always a good      |
| option when you get in trouble just remember that there are quite a few      |
| stops where you must fight. After the final stop begin to pummel Octienne.   |
| Keep dodging his attacks use stuns to keep him locked down.                  |

|==============================================================================|

 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  Alyn Shir wanted you to meet her in Emaire and it's going to be quite the
venture from anything you've likely discovered. Fast Travel as close as you can
and start the journey. As you enter the Plains of Erathell you can find a
graveyard with a [STONE OF THE WOLDS] inside. You should also pass by the
village of Ayten for an easy travel location. If you stick to the road you will
find another [STONE OF THE WOLDS] just before moving into the Forsaken Plain.
Be on the lookout for Freeman Assassins, they tend to ambush along the roads.

  Continue north and the main road leads straight into Emaire. Enter the Blue
Bear Tavern and speak with Alyn Shir. The poor General is still in exile and is
fated to never succeed. You must head to Urul-Tusk in the Cradle of Summer to
the northwest. As you follow the road north you can spot a [CRADLE OF SUMMER
STONE] off the right side of the path; there is also another just before you
cross into the zone itself. A third [CRADLE OF SUMMER STONE] can be found if you
go west as soon as you enter the zone near a jump point.

N o t e
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  There is a Hidden Door in this zone that leads to rare items. To find this,
head east of Urul Tusk, just on the other side of the river. Follow the path and
loot the hidden object for the [SKILL BOOK (ALCHEMY)] then jump down to find a
[GRAVE] by itself with [KHAS-TI'S HELM].

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  When you finally reach Urul-Tusk speak with General Tilera. Accept the [ERATHI
WINDCHIME] and use it on the Ancient Windstone to the west. A Niskaru
Bloodhunter will strike when the windstone is struck so be ready for the fight.
You are left with the task of finding the other four Ancient Windstones and
striking them to open the gate. Do this however you wish, just know that without
Fast Travelling it could take some time.

  The Windstone in Tala-Rane will summon two Niskaru and is in the central part
of this zone. South of Caer Tosai is where you will find the Kandrian Windstone.
In the northeast corner of Acatha the Windstone will summon four Niskaru
Bloodhunters after you; there is also a [CHEST] and [WHIRPOOL] nearby. The
final Windchime in the Forsaken plain will bring about a Niskaru Tyrant. Be
careful as this one can be dangerous. Behind the stone you can loot [KALLAS'
NOTES] and then be on your way back to the Urul-Tusk. A disturbance occurs and
you are teleported to the Deep Slumber. You have broken the barrier and you can
restore it, but those side quests can be accomplished at your leisure.

  Return to Urul-Tusk and go inside, moving west through the narrow pathway.
As you approach a fork in the road three Niskaru spawn to ambush you. There is
a locked [CHEST] to the north, grab it before continuing west. As you approach a
staircase turn left and loot the [CHEST] at the end of the corridor. Move down
the steps and kill three more Niskaru and loot the [CHEST] in the southeastern
corner. Head west and two Niskaru Hunters come running into the room where a
[CHEST] also resides.

  Go through the winding chasms south and then eventually back north where you
will find Giant Rats. Beyond the rats is a room with two [CHESTS] and a hidden
passageway going east -- use the Erathi Sigil-Stone to progress. Two more
Niskaru Hunters lurk in this room as well as a [CHEST]. Get ready for a tough
fight before progressing up the stairs.

|  After the short scene two Niskaru Hunters strike at you. When these two are |

| appearance once these Niskaru fall. At melee range the beast can use a tail  |
| spin that knocks you back a ways. Azaghaal can also stretch his arms and     |
| cause magical damage to you as well as shoot frost breath and fire balls     |
| from his mouth. The charge attack will leave you stunned but dodging it      |
| leaves the foe open. The best attacks to counter are the frost breath and    |
| charge so focus on closing the distance with a dodge roll. Azaghaal can be   |
| stunned and paralyzed but it's very infrequent. Stick to dodging and         |
| countering when Azaghaal is still using his attacks.                         |

{{{
  Make the journey to Rathir and head to the Upper City. Get Elund Carth to
send troops with you to Mel Senshir, if you pass the Persuasion Check you can
even leave with [ELUND'S RING]. Go back down the steps and to the dock to sail
to Mel Senshir. Speak with Commander Owaiglyn upon your arrival. Listen to the
plan he has to unravel the Tuatha and talk to him again once you are ready.

  Begin your onslaught heading north taking out a single Tuatha Soldier then
a group of three. Go up the steps and through the gate, turning right to grab
a [CHEST]. There are two more locked [CHESTS] in this room but you might not
have time to loot them before two Tuatha Priests enter to ruin your day. Watch
out for the traps in the next corridor. It's not difficult to dodge roll by
them if you know they are there. At the balcony you need to break the siege
ladders and fight off the Tuatha with Alyn Shir.

  In the next area the path is split, go whichever way you want and try to
save your comrades. Open the door and cut through the enemies on the next
balcony, but don't forget to cut down the siege ladder. You can find five
[CHESTS] and a Blacksmithing Forge in the next room. Utilize whatever you need
and head out to the Ramparts. Slay the few Tuatha that are in your way then
head down the path for a dual with the Witch Knight Malwyn.

| attack combination cannot be broken like normal characters but he is very    |
| susceptible to stun and paralyze. Spells like Ice Barrage, Storm Bolt, and   |
| Quake can give you some breathing room and time to execute some combos of    |
| your own. Malwyn has a massive amount of health and will periodically Blink  |
| to a distance tower. At this time you need to face the Balor and block with  |
| your shield in order to survive. Continue to dodge and melee Malwyn or keep  |
| your distance and use stuns until his health is depleted.                    |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |

  After the scene loot Malwyn and enter the Battlements. Fight off the Tuatha
with Agarth's assistance then continue north to fight off three more soldiers.
Loot the [CHEST] then head up the steps and clear the balcony. Head back inside
to find more Tuatha then go through the gate to find a Prismere Troll. Clear
the room and loot the [CHEST] then head out to an overhang. The Balor is firing
his laser eye in a semi-circle here. You can dodge it and grab the [CHEST]
contents then dart into the next area.

  Slay the Tuatha Zealots and enter a fierce fight with a Tuatha Priest and
a Niskaru Tyrant. Kill the priest first and use stuns to keep the Tyrant back.
Head out to the Ramparts to start the fight against the monstrous Balor.

|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |

are several Tuatha Raiders here and nothing more. After the short conversation
with Gadflow, break the crystal and be on your way to the next Chantry in the
southeast corner. You'll find much of the same here, destroy the crystals and
be on your way to the northeastern corner of The Keening. Return to Cydan to

Continue east up the stairs to find another group of Laz.

you will encounter a mixture of Faer Gorta and Sons of Laz. There is a locked
[CHEST] in the back corner that you should open before continuing.

to a room with four [CHESTS] and the note [THE NEW ASSISTANT]. Meet Ventrinio

Gorta and Ancient Leanashe will join the fray the longer you hold out and
Ventrinio will start to aid you. Talk with Ventrinio after you've completed the
task to receive the [SOUL LENS] and complete the quest.

junction of the north and south parts. Stick to the main road and at the fork
you can find another [CAELED COAST STONE]. Continue east and kill the Borgan
Brutes and check the the west side of cliff for another [CAELED COAST STONE]
then head to the House of Pride..

  Meet with Dren and fight a quick and pointless battle. There is a Persuasion
Check during the speech but all options point to a fight to the death.

 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                                    Dren                                      |
|                                                                              |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|  Dren is a Fighter and uses high tier skills in that area. His combos are    |
| sluggish however and easily avoided and countered. A favored technique is    |
| the Comet Strike but it takes so long to charge up that you can stun him.    |
| Keeping distance is easy and Storm Bolt provides an easy stun. Reckoning     |
| isn't necessary but use it if you want to speed things up. Dren will use a   |
| teleporting ability and strengthen himself with War Cry so have some ranged  |
| skills handy to stop him from buffing up.                                    |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Check out the [STONE OF WINTER] after the battle and speak with Agarth. Enter
the House of Pride and fight alongside the Allies. Kill the three Tuatha Priests
in the first room then prepare for a larger group in the next. Loot the [CHEST]
and head into the next room where a Bolgan Brute and Tuatha Overlord await with
their lackies. The Overlord can present a challenge so focus on him first. Loot
the two [CHESTS] and enter the next room where a solo [CHEST] lies.

  Up the stairs the Knave of Pride stops you then asks you to slay the Witch
Knight Myrna.

 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                             Witch Knight Myrna                               |
|                                                                              |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|  While technically a boss, the Witch Knight Myrna shouldn't ever pose too    |
| much of a threat. What little health she has can be easily drained of her.   |
| She can summon a Faer Gorta to assist her but ignore it and try to lock her  |
| up in melee where her attacks are naught. It is possible to infinitely combo |
| Myrna to death and that is the suggested method of defeat.                   |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Head east and kill the two Tuatha Soldiers then bust the crystals to have yet
another talk with Gadflow. Talk with the Knave of Pride once more to conclude
the quest and obtain the [TWIST OF FATE - UNSTOPPABLE FORCE].

}}}
 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|                              Taking Vengeance                     [06.13.00] |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ITEMS:      None                                                             |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| EQUIPMENT:  Reprisal's Gauntlets     [ ]  Retribution's Greaves          [ ] |
|             Vengeance's Cuirass      [ ]  Vindication's Chausses         [ ] |
|             Wrath's Helm             [ ]                                     |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ENEMIES:    Arcane Barghest               Cur of Vengeance*                  |
|             Elite Murghan                 Faer Gorta                         |
|             Gadflow*                      Niskaru Bloodhunter                |
|             Niskaru Hunter                Prismere Troll                     |
|             Sprite                        Tuatha Overlord                    |
|             Tuatha Priest                 Tuatha Soldier                     |
|             Tuatha Zealot                                                    |
|______________________________________________________________________________|
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  Make your exit into Alabastra and talk to Alyn Shir. Move down the road into
Camp Moondown, if you go west and north past it you can find an [ALABASTRA
STONE]. Follow the road until you run into Ventrinio again who briefs you.
Check the [STONE OF WINTER] and loot the [CHEST] to the south then continue
along the road. Enter Shadow Pass and fight off the Tuatha as you will pass
another [ALABASTRA STONE].

  Further along, before you leave Shadow Pass, a Prismere Troll impedes your
path. It can still be difficult so be sure to exercise all necessary precautions
while fighting it. South from here you can meet Cydan and find a third
[ALABASTRA STONE]. Down the road you can find Witch Knight Dessidyn in the
camp. Enter the Twilight Pass and slay the few Tuatha that ambush you before
snagging another [ALABASTRA STONE]. Pass through Ashmoor and turn north to find
a few Sprites and another [STONE OF WINTER]. Just past the Eventide you can find
the final [ALABASTRA STONE] . Turn the corner of the long path to meet Cydan
who is in turn waiting for Agarth, who seems to show up right on time.

  Alyn Shir is missing, but the group is ready when you are. Fight your way to
the top of the hill where you can find a [STONE OF WINTER] sitting before the
entrance to the House of Vengeance. Kill the Tuatha and continue to follow the
group to another group of Tuatha. The next group you fight is a somewhat
elaborate room where you can find two [CHESTS]. There isn't much of note until
you reach the top and face the Cur of Vengeance.

 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                              Cur of Vengeance                                |
|                                                                              |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|  The Cur of Vengeance will fight much like Dren, so use the previous fight   |
| a guideline. When the Cur does the teleport he will summon Niskaru to join   |
| the fight in addition to the Tuatha Zealots that are already present. Set    |
| your focus on the additional enemies before taking on the Cur. With the help |
| of the others this battle should go smoothly.                                |
|                                                                              |
| Drops: Vengeance's Cuirass, Vindication's Chausses, Wrath's Helm             |
|        Reprisal's Gauntlets, Retribution's Greaves                           |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Loot the three [CHESTS] then go south to find another two [CHESTS] before
entering Bhaile. Speak with Alyn Shir and check the [BHAILE STONE] then go down
the pathway. Slay the Niskaru and find the next [BHAILE STONE]. Cross the
bridge and slay a few more Tuatha as the third [BHAILE STONE] is on this island.
Around the bend you will face a Prismere Troll and find the fourth [BHAILE
STONE] along with another [STONE OF WINTER]. The final [BHAILE STONE] is in the
northwest corner before you reach the Court of Winter, there is also a [CHEST]
just before you reach the court.

 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                                   Gadflow                                    |
|                                                                              |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|  Gadflow will immediately clone himself at the start of the battle. The best |
| way to know which one to attack is the one that Alyn Shir is attacking.      |
| Gadflow knows all the magic spells there are and then some! At certain times |
| he will lay traps all along the floor and strike you are range. Do your best |
| to close the distance and get some shots in. Block the fireballs and unleash |
| a combo to get the ball rolling again. Be sure to kill the clones then focus |
| on the real Gadflow. It is possible to continually knockback Gadflow with    |
| power strikes but stunning and paralyzing is difficult and rare to come by.  |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Foiled! Alyn Shir says there is no time to waste but four [CHESTS] beg to
differ. The quest ends and the final battle is nigh.

}}}
 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|                                  Reckoning                        [06.14.00] |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ITEMS:      Twist of Fate - Destiny Defiant [ ]                              |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| EQUIPMENT:  None                                                             |
|                                                                              |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ENEMIES:    Splinter of Fate             Tirnoch*                            |
|______________________________________________________________________________|
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  Go west and enter Amethyn where you will fight a Splinter of Fate, a replica
of you. Loot the [CHEST] and go north to find another one in an alcove to the
right. Fight another Splinter of Fate and dispel the [CHEST] as you move west.
There are several items on the table as you turn the corner to fight another
Splinter of Fate. Continue along the path and fight double Fates then open the
two [CHESTS] and continue north to another one. Enter the Throne Room to view a
scene and square off against Tirnoch.
}}}
 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                                   Tirnoch                                    |
|                                                                              |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|  Tirnoch will create Splinters of Fate from you. Slay them and use Reckoning |
| when ever your bar is full. This will drop Tirnoch in front of you and allow |
| you to damage her. You will transition to a new island every time you deal   |
| 1/4 of her life bar and one additional Splinter of Fate will emerge. Be sure |
| dodge Tirnoch's attacks as you fight off the Splinters, but it shouldn't be  |
| too incredibly difficult.                                                    |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  You receive the [TWIST OF FATE - DESTINY DEFIANT] and the game has ended, or
has it? There is much to do in the world of Amalur and the main quest is just
the tip of the iceberg.
}}}
 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|                                  Primordia                        [06.15.00] |
|==============================================================================|
|                                                                              |
| ENEMIES:    Arcane Barghest              Banshaen Princess                   |
|             Chicken Overlord             Elite Murghan                       |
|             Prismere Troll               Sprite                              |
|______________________________________________________________________________|
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  After defeating Tirnoch you can enter the lair of Primordia in High Fulgen.
Slay the Arcane Barghest in the first room and dispel the [FAE CACHE]. Go north
east and kill the Sprites then open the Hidden Door. Slay the Chicken Overlords
then continue north through the Sprites and Arcane Barghest. Slay the enemies
in this large central room then move west. Kill the Sprites and search the next
room for a [FAE CACHE]. Go down the ramp to the far western room and defeat the
Prismere Troll. Loot the [CHEST] and the [FAE CACHE] to complete the dungeon.

}}}

                       |          Side Quests           |             [07.00.00]

                       |________________________________|            
                        ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
  There are a lot of Side Quests and Tasks that you can acquire during your time
in Amalur. They are listed in the zone that you can acquire them so you don't
miss any while passing through.

================================================================================
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                    ODARATH                           [07.01.00]
________________________________________________________________________________
================================================================================
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Crisis of Faith
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Father Dynwel
Location:    Gorhart

  Start this quest after clearing the Red Legion Camps in Recipe for Trouble.
To the west of the last camp you can spot several Brownies. Slay them and move
south to find a hollow log leading into the central area. Help Brother Egan
kill the Boggarts then speak with him. Agree to help then follow him to
Waterhall Downs. There is a [LOOT PILE] to the north, but proceed in the other
direction. Slay the Boggarts and move through the watery area, don't bypass the
[WHIRLPOOL] that is sure to reap rewards. At the end of the watery passageway
is a [LOOT PILE] containing [350 COINS] and [AMMAN'S KEY - AUTUMN]. Moving near
the pile unfortunately summons Sprites that surround you.

  Further along you will encounter more Sprites and a [CHEST]. This chest has
traps all around it so be careful. Your reward is the [SELKIE VEIL] and a few
more Sprites that appear to guard the treasure. To the right of this chest is
another [CHEST] hidden behind some pots. Exit back into Odarath and loot the
[CHEST] before jumping down. When you return to the camp and talk to the "Fae"
you can pass a Persuasion Check to avoid combat, but either option lets you keep
the Veil.

  Follow Brother Egan back to the mission and unlock the [CHEST] to the left as
you enter the newly opened gate. Speak with the Father to receive your reward.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               Building Bridges
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Herc Adwold
Location:    Gorhart - Town Center

  Head north of Gorhart and turn west when you get the chance. Hug the wall
and you'll find a locked [CHEST] and some Wolves. You have the chance to go
south but avoid it for now. Kill the Boggarts guarding the Shrine of Thyrdon
then move north across the stream to find an [ODARATH STONE]. Return to the
southern area and speak with Aery. Craft or purchase the Greater Healing Potion
then speak with Herc Adwold. He wants you to go to the House of Ballads and
speak with the Fae. You can lie and say that you saved the maiden from a group
of bandits to win favor.

  Return to Herc Adwold when you have completed this task to receive your just
reward.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              Recipe for Trouble
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Nanne Hanri
Location:    Gorhart - Golden Age Alchemy

  Leave town with the quests you have at the first opening along the road turn
right and button hook to find a [CHEST] with the weapons, armor, and an
[ANONYMOUS JOURNAL]. There are Brownies and some Boggarts in this area but they
should go down swiftly. An [ALTAR OF BELEN] is near the Boggarts and further
south an [ODARATH STONE]. Enter Agnur Farhal and open the door along the path.
To the left you can spot Karth Hilfred, but first destroy the crates and unlock
the [CHEST].

  Karth has deceived Nanne and the Red Legion are striking against you! Quickly
dispatch them and move east along the path. Fight off the Red Legion and destroy
the crates as you move onward. At the crossroads head north to find Brownies
hovering over a [CORPSE] and a [STONE OF AUTUMN] in the corner. You can find
much of the same along the southern part of the crossroad with the addition of
a [CHEST]. To continue this quest, make your way east and down the steps where
four Red Legion members wait. Slay them and destroy two more crates then unlock
the [CHEST] and use the [STONE OF AUTUMN]. Up the steps you exit into Odarath
where a [CHEST] sits nearby. Jump down and head to the far north, across the
road.

  Along the western edge you will find a Red Legion Camp where you must slay
the enemies and destroy the crates. Loot the [ABANDONED PACK] to find [AMMAN'S
KEY - WINTER] and [SIGBERT'S JOURNAL]. Move up to the next camp and search for a
[HIDDEN DOOR]. There is a [DISPEL CHEST] behind this hidden door. In the camp
above this one is a locked [CHEST] and a [DALENTARTH STONE]. Cross the stream
and search the [WHIRLPOOL] for some items then lay waste to the camps. Of note
in this camp is Osgar Krast who drops [OSGAR KRAST'S BLADE]. There is a [CHEST]
on the east side of the camp near the crates and another along with an
[OVERTURNED CART] near the northern crates. Return to Nanne to receive several
[POTIONS] and some robes.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Members Only
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Sister Zelda
Location:    Gorhart - Chapel Gates
Requirement: Complete Crisis of Faith

  After completing Crisis of Faith, leave the chapel area and speak with Sister
Zelda. She wants you to enter the Order of Mitharu and acquire an Ordination
Tome. Enter St. Odwig's Reliquary and take the [ORDINATION RITES]. There are two
[CHESTS] that you can easily steal from in this room if you want. The task
[BROTHER TIL'S COLLECTION] starts if you browse it. The collection can be found
in the main foyer of St. Odwig's Reliquary. In the basement you can speak with
Brother Delf to start [OUT OF THE PAST]. Leave the reliquary and head up towards
the Chapel. Loot the [CHEST] along the left side and return to Zelda for your
reward.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Long Overdue
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Brother Til's Bookshelf
Location:    Gorhart - Reliquary
Requirement: Complete Crisis of Faith

Til's Collection I    - Found in Vorm Lodge on a bookshelf in the back corner.
Til's Collection II   - Inside the Mayor's House in Whitestone.
Til's Collection III  - Found in the Vauner House in Canneroc in the basement.
Til's Collection IV   - In a locked chest at the Moon Camp.
Til's Collection V    - Second floor of Luminitsa's Cottage south of Didenhil.
Til's Collection VI   - In the Dormitory outside the Scholia Arcana in Rathir.
Til's Collection VII  - In the Livrarium in Adessa.
Til's Collection VIII - In the Livrarium in Adessa
Til's Collection IX   - In the Edmure home in Emaire.
Til's Collection X    - In Castle Ansilla in the Caeled Coast.

  After tracking down all 10 books return to the bookshelf to receive a very
miniscule amount of gold. All that hard work for nothing!

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Out of the Past
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Brother Delf
Location:    Gorhart - Reliquary
Requirement: Complete Crisis of Faith

  You are tasked with acquiring the daggers of two former colleagues of Brother
Delf. The first one, Ugnar Odgray, can be found behind the Inn at Gorhart.
Simply persuade him to hand the dagger over and you avoid any confrontation.
Head out east to the area between Glendara and Haxhi to find Itran the Shade.
Enter the Bloodstone Deep and kill the first wave of Red Legion Raiders. at the
fork turn left to find a locked [CHEST] and on the right two more Red Legion.

  In the next fork both the left and right sides have Red Legion but the left
only has a [CHEST] (the right has a hidden Hollow Log). Go down the center and
kill the rest of the Red Legion until you get a chance to speak with Red. At
this point you can kill Red or side with him and kill Delf. Brother Delf will
give you [BROTHER DELF'S KEY] so you can unlock his [CHEST].

}}}

                             Red in Tooth and Claw
