 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Ainmhi
Location:    Along the road in the west side of east Odarath

  Move west from Ainmhi to find the Sprites, all elemental, emerge from the
ground to ambush you. Defeat them and return to Ainmhi who needs you to fix
the well's water. Move south past Penri Kell then turn west to find the Well.
You receive the [DRAUGHT OF THE WANDERING WELL] for your efforts but you must
give it to Ainmhi to complete the quest, and there's no reward!

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                  Homecoming
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Gizela Wulflac
Location:    Gorhart - Graveyard
Requirement: Complete Building Bridges

  Speak with Gizela Wulflac to discover she has been waiting for her husband
Camden to return. Make your way east to the village of Didenhil in the area of
Glendara. You can also find the [DEATH NOTICE: CAMDEN WULFLAC] and tell Gizela
about it, it can be found in the center of west Odarath on a corpse, though she
denies that he is dead anyways. Enter the Three Lamps Inn at Didenhil and talk
some sense into Camden. Return to Gizela for your reward as the quest completes.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             The Statues of Amman
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: N/A
Location:    East Odarath

  While not listed in the quest log, you can acquire four different keys to
open the four Statues of Amman located in the east half of Odarath. The first
key you can find is at the Corner Shop, you have to buy [AMMAN'S KEY - WINTER]
or find it in one of the Red Legion Camps. The [AMMAN'S KEY - AUTUMN] is found
during the quest Crisis of Faith in the Waterhall Downs. [AMMAN'S KEY - SPRING]
can be found in the House of Ballads' Summer Sanctuary in a [CHEST]. [AMMAN'S
KEY - SUMMER] can be found in the House of Ballad's House of Accolades. Journey
to the four corners of east Odarath and you will find one Amman Statue in each.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             The Flame of Rhyderk
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Echostone
Location:    House of Ballads - Hall of Accolades

  Pick up [THE FLAME OF RHYDERK] near Glianal and the Echostone (to his right
on the ground). Use the Echostone to start the quest then go south of the
Warden Bridge in Lorca-Rane and clear out the Jutton so you can loot [RHYDERK'S
BLADE]. Go to a Blacksmith Forge and create the Greatsword [RHYDERK].

}}}

                              Reprisal, Reprised
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Penri Kell
Location:    At the ruins as you cross from Odarath into Yolvan.

  Talk with Penri to learn about a Troll that stole some valuables. Slay a few
Antelope to get their heads. Return to Penri then mount them in the ruins to
draw out Lekka the Corpulent, a Troll. Slay the beast and loot the [MAIDEN'S
RING]. If you convince Penri then you can keep it, but otherwise you must fight
her for it.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Ungentle Beasts
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Contract Board
Location:    Shieldring Keep

  Head to the southwest corner of east Odarath to find the Overgrown Thicket.
In the first area you can find three Kobolds and a [CHEST]. Go west to find two
Barghest and another [CHEST], this one isn't locked. The final area has five
Kobolds, three [CHESTS] and [THE BOOK OF GENTLE BEASTS] resting on a rock.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               A Brutal Contract
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Contract Board
Location:    Shieldring Keep

  Talk to Declan Malus to discover there are five Trolls that need slaying.
Check your quest markers to see there is one just west of your current location.
Don't miss looting [JORY'S CORPSE] before going south to find another Troll only
a short distance away. Continue south along the road to find a third Troll then
begin moving east. As you approach Splitrock Depths you will find the fourth
Troll. The last Troll can be found northwest of Splitrock. When the last one is
slain return to Declan Malus to receive your reward.


}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Rallying Cry
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Contract Board
Location:    Shieldring Keep

  You are tasked with slaying the Ettin Shamans in Ettinmere. You can find them
at the following locations:

Sul    - Camp in the southeast along the road
Merog  - Middle island
Duxtir - In the northern-most camp
Ansir  - Southern-most area near the Ballads Oratory.

  After slaying the Ettin Shaman head to Shieldring Keep to report the news.

}}}

                                Knowledge Lost
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Oleander Sinclair
Location:    Camp - East of Shieldring Keep

  You receive [RECIPE - MINOR ALCHEMIST'S ART] if you don't have it. This will
show you how to make the potion that Oleander wants, but you can always just
head into Shieldring Keep and find it. Return to Oleander to receive a bunch of
gold as your reward.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             The Treasures of Meropis
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Echostone
Location:    Ballads Library

  Play the Treasures of Meropis found in the Ballads Library to start this
quest. You are tasked with finding a few treasures across Dalentarth.

- Northern river of west Odarath near the last Red Legion Camp.
- South of Didenhil in the middle of the lake.
- At Warden's Bridge near the waterfall in the river.
- Northwest of the Ballads Oratory in the river.
- In the river between Dellach and Holnstead.

  Once you have found the last item the quest completes.

}}}

                                   Glendara                           [07.03.00]
________________________________________________________________________________
================================================================================

 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               The Natural Order
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
Quest Giver: Thaddeus Holn
Location:    Outside of Didenhil

  Help Thaddeus by slaying the Boggart that is attacking him. Agree to help and
talk to Kester Barclay in the middle of the city. He suggests that you head
north to Coilsbain Caverns and defeat the Jottun there to help dissolve the
plague. Head north and enter the cavern, making your way to a small camp with
two Jottun. Treat these foes like mini-trolls as they will use charge attacks
and close range smashes. Stuns work well for setting them up to die. Once the
Jottun are defeated loot the [CHEST] and head down the hall.

  Open the door at the end of the hallway to find a Boggart and a [CHEST]. Go
east and find a [CHEST] at the northern end near the waterfall then continue
your march until you meet two more Boggarts and another [CHEST]. Around the bend
you'll encounter another pair of Jottun, but the next area houses three of the
beasts to include a Chieftain. Pop open the [CHESTS] on the western side then
head north where you can find a third and the entrance to the Coilsbain Ruins.

  There is a [CHEST] by the waterfall so don't miss it before heading through
the elegant door. Fight off a singular Jottun then slay the final two on a
circular platform around the corner. Go through the next door and slay the mage
Balthasar. Ignore the Faer Gorta as he continues to summon them and they all
disappear once he is slain anyways. Read the [ANCIENT TOME] and loot the [CHEST]
before turning to Kester Barclay. Your reward is [EVALYNE'S RING] as the quest
comes to a close.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Plagueshield
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Astrid Frisk
Location:    Outside Three Lamps Inn at Didenhil

  Talk to Astrid to learn that the cure for the plague hasn't arrived yet. Go
out in search of Brother Fallon to the west of Didenhil to discover several Red
Legion Raiders around a cart. Slay them and loot the [CORPSE] to find [ST.
HADWYN'S BEADS] and a letter [TO BROTHER FALLON II], search the cart for some
[PLAGUESHIELD]. Head north from here and follow the Red Legion Scout back to a
camp on the east side of Glendara. Slay the Red Legion and loot the corpse to
find a second [PLAGUESHIELD]. North of Bloodstone Deep where you tracked the
Red Legion Scout you can find the final [PLAGUESHIELD].

  Return to Astrid to receive your reward of four [GREATER HEALING POTIONS].
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                            Brother Fallon's Beads
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Brother Udo
Location:    St. Hadwyn's Mission

  Brother Udo is in search of Brother Fallon but you've likely found his corpse
down the road with the [ST. HADWYN'S BEADS] attached. If not head south and grab
them and return to Udo. If you worship Mitharu, or lie, you can keep the beads
otherwise you are given a few potions.

}}}

                               The Natural Order

 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Murdoc Hain
Location:    Didenhil - Crafting Shop

  Murdoc needs Fire Damage Potions or Tindertwig and Scarwood Bark to make the
potions. This quest is repeatable and offers gold as a reward.

}}}

                                    Webwood                           [07.04.00]

 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 A Tangled Web
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Garaner Vernt
Location:    Canneroc

  Slay the Giant Spiders and Venomspitters in Canneroc then talk to Garaner to
get things rolling. Meet him on the southern end of the village, accept his
offer, and head to the southwest portion of Webwood and into the Shade River
Caves. Down the path you will encounter four Venomspitters and at the split in
the road, another three. Go north at this split to meet Barten who is fighting
off several Giant Spiders. Tell him of Garaner's betrayal and return to
Canneroc. Your reward is the [KEY TO GOSSAMER END], your new mansion in the
city.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Gossamer End
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Barten
Location:    Canneroc

  Simply enter your house and then visit Billis Aideh in the Silken Seat to see
what upgrades you can make to the place. Each upgrade costs approximately 500
gold.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Cutting the Threads
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Barten
Location:    Canneroc
Requirement: Complete A Tangled Web
  
  Venture to the northwest corner of Webwood to find Castle Yolvan. The normal
entrance is destroyed so go around the corner and jump down. Search the [YOLVAN
STONE] in the initial room and head north. At the end of this hall is another
[YOLVAN STONE]. Enter the main halls and go straight across, following this path
to another [YOLVAN STONE]. At the end of the hall is a [CHEST], loot it and go
west. Defeat the Giant Rats and scope out the [SPIDER SAC] as you enter the west
corner. Watch out for the deceptive venus fly trap if you attempt to harvest the
reagent.

  Just south you will find the fourth [YOLVAN STONE] and a group of Giant Rats.
Head west and south to the final [YOLVAN STONE] then move towards The Widow.
Don't pass up the [SPIDER SACS] and [SKELETONS] along the way, they can hold
valuable items. The Widow leaves as Giant Spiders and Venomspitters appear. If
you have Mark of Flame now would be an optimal time to use it, though you could
also use Reckoning and collect a large amount of experience.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               The Widow's Wrath
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: The Widow
Location:    Castle Yorvan
Requirement: Complete Cutting the Threads

  Start backtracking and watch out for the Venomspitters that spawn in the
hallway. In the first large room you reach a group of Giant Spiders will ambush
you. The same thing applies for the next two larger rooms as you return to the
middle. Go northwest and unlock the gate and fight off the Giant Rats to find a
[CHEST] and [SPIDER SAC] worth looting. Head straight across the hall and kill
the last Venomspitters on your back to Yolvan. As you enter the village a group
of spiders spawns and you must defend the citizens.

  With some guidance from Barten, head south to Cathrus. The Widow presents the
option of wiping out Canneroc, but choose not to. Go south and fight off the
Venomspitters and in the hallway use a staff/sceptre to break the web and reach
a locked [CHEST]. In the nearby room you will encounter a few waves of spiders
so be ready to continually fight and back into the hallway if you need to
funnel them down. Follow the zigzag path southwest and break the web at the
turning point to find a [SPIDER SAC].

  The path leads southwest still to another room full of spiders. Just outside
this room is a web that you can break to reach another [SPIDER SAC] and as you
move northwest you can find another one. Follow the path as you slay the spiders
until you face off with The Widow.


 ______________________________________________________________________________

|                                  The Widow                                   |

|  The Widow just continually summons more Giant Spiders and Venomspitters so  |
| your biggest concern is keeping her locked down. This can be difficult since |
| she teleports often and the spiders can become overwhelming. Use the area of |
| effect attacks that you have, but stick to Mark of Flame if you have it. Try |
| to stun The Widow with Storm Bolt and let her have it. If the battle starts  |
| to become too difficult use Reckoning to slow things down and turn the tide  |
| of battle in your favor. As she falls under 50% health The Widow will keep   |
| at range and start casting at you, so keep the pressure up and use potions.  |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Loot the corpse and the [CHEST] at the north end before returning to Barten
in Canneroc. Your reward is a hefty sum of gold and [CANNEROC GOSSAMER x2].
}}}

                               Resting the Bones
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Silkfarmer Remains
Location:    Scattered in Webwood

  Find the remains of the six unfortunate Silkfarmers:

- Northeast corner just south of the Ironhold Passage.
- In a camp in the south west corner of Webwood, north of Shade River Caves.
- Just off the road from Canneroc going west.
- Off the southern path into Haxhi.
- Continue down the road to spot this corpse in webs near a tree.
- On a cliff just north of Cathrus in southeastern Webwood.

  With all the remains, return to the west side of Canneroc and inspect the
Ossuary to place the bones and receive a chunk of experience.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Grim Harvest
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Menri Togh
Location:    Canneroc

  Menri is worried about her family at Togh Farm, so venture to the southeast
corner of Webwood. Slay the Giant Spiders and Venomspitters outside the house
and loot the locked [CHEST] before heading inside. Search the [SPIDER SACS] and
corpses then head down the steps to find [JAYCK'S KNIFE]. Head back to Webwood
and approach Cartery about the corpses. You can take the payoff or confront him,
which leads to the better reward. Slay Cartery and return to Menri to receive a
nice sum of gold and the unique [SILKFARMER GLOVES].
}}}

                                Hair of the Dog
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Syllareta Vauner
Location:    The Silken Seat
Requirement: Complete The Widow's Wrath

  Find Syllareta at the inn to discover she needs some supplies to fill her
store again. Head out into Webwood and kill any Giant Spiders you find in hopes
of getting a [POISON GLAND]. Return to Syllareta once you have obtained 15 of
them to receive some [MINOR VENOMGUARD]. You can periodically check back in
with Syllareta and she will give you more potions free of charge.

}}}

                             The Fisherman's Bride
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Enconeg Holn
Location:    Holnstead

  Enconeg Holn is in search of his bride but she never came so he wants you to
clear the monsters out from around the area in hopes that she returns. Start
at the dock to the east where a pack of Wolves sits. Kill them and head south
up the ramp and kill the Ettin Brute. Follow him to the "Nymph" which is just a
Leanashe. Kill the beast and you will be rewarded with [ENCONEG'S RING].
}}}

                                Imelda's Charm
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Enconeg Holn
Location:    Holnstead
Requirement: Complete The Fisherman's Bride

  Follow the southern road towards Dellach and you will encounter an Ettin Brute
that will drop [IMELDA'S CHARM]. Return to Enconeg for your reward, a sum of
gold.
}}}

                               Shine and Shadow
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Avicenn Etelle
Location:    Holnstead

  Talk to Avicenn in Holnstead and make a beeline for Dellach in search of Shine
and Shadow. After you pass the Codex of Destiny and return to Dellach from the
Theatre of Fate you encounter a group of Ettin, among them Kurtorix. Slay the
beast and loot [SHINE AND SHADOW]. Convince Avicenn to let you keep the daggers
and receive compensation in gold to end the quest.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              Shadow of Enfamanir
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Echostone
Location:    Ballads Oratory

  Pick up the [SHADOW OF ENFAMANIR] inside the Ballads Oratory, just to the left
of the Echostone. Use the Echostone and accept the ballad then head to the south
east corner of the Sidhe. Slay Enfamanir the Niskaru Tyrant with frost-based
spells and loot the corpse for some goods.

}}}

                                 The Flowering

{{{
Quest Giver: Osduin
Location:    Northwest of Brunuath

  Osduin needs you to gather the Chrysalae around Lorca-Rane. Enter Brunuath
and find Osduin who wants you to plant some seeds. Return the center platform
and fight off a huge wave of Sprites. Osduin is displeased and attacks you
after a short conversation with a smaller wave of Sprites. Kill them all and the
quest completes, Osduin can be looted for a [GEM OF CULTIVATION].
}}}

{{{
Quest Giver: Jedda Kerning
Location:    Warden's Bridge

  Jedda is looking for her comrades, one of them named Turin. Head to the east
side of Lorca-Rane, south of Brunuath, to find a corpse with a [SEALED CONTRACT]
on it. Return the Jedda to complete the quest.

  Release this man from his cage and seek out the Marga at a nearby camp to the

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              The Height of Crime
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Stellan Reitan
Location:    West of Splitrock Depths

  Stellan has concern for his friend so enter the nearby Splitrock Depths in
search of him. Go north at the split and at the joint area in the middle kill
the Faer Gorta. Double around to the other half of the split to find some
Barghest and a [SKELETON] in the dead end; there is a [CHEST] off the main path
as well. Return to the center area and go southeast to find more Barghest.
Follow the path and turn left at the juncture if you wish to slay more of the
foul beasts.

  Further along you will find more Faer Gorta and a [CHEST] tucked in the west
alcove. Enter the final room then loot Despero for [THE JOURNAL OF STELLAN
REITAN] and search the cage for [A TATTERED JOURNAL]. As you start to leave a
Leanashe appears to halt you. Slay her and leave, but take the other exit along
the north path that you came in on. Outside you can find Brother Padric's corpse
with [BROTHER PADRIC'S TRAVEL NOTES] on it as well as a [CHEST]. Stellan rewards
you with some gold for returning his journal.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             Band of Brother Monks
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Brother Padric's Corpse
Location:    Secondary exit of Splitrock Depths

  You can find the travel notes that start this quest during The Height of
Crime. Head to St. Eadric's Mission in the Sidhe just past the Star Camp to find
Brother Holt. If you enter the Bunkhouse and enter the basement you can find a
[CHEST] with a [DESK KEY]. Return to the first floor and use it on Father
Etair's Desk to acquire a [STORAGE CASE].

}}}

                              Aggressive Brownies
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Sihtric Vorm
Location:    Vorm Lodge

  Talk to Sihtric Vorm in the Vorm Lodge to hear about Brownies that have been
ambushing folks along the road. Head to the southeast near a wrecked cart and
slay the Brownies and loot the corpses. Return to Sihtric for your reward.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                The Brownie Den
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Sihtric Vorm
Location:    Vorm Lodge
Requirement: Complete Aggressive Brownies

  Sihtric wants to investigate the behavior of the Brownies. Head to Rundamir
in the south and clear the initial room of Brownies. Loot the [CHEST] at the
southeast then go south to a dead end where a Browni can be found. Down the
other half of this path is a group of Brownies and a dispel [CHEST] in the south
east corner. Continue southwest and take the turn at the fork to a door where a
[CHEST] can be found.

  At the end of the southern path you will find the Crudok. Do your best to
dodge the poison it throws and stun it. After it dies the quest completes but
you can still explore the other half of the dungeon. Go northwest and slay some
Brownies then dispel the [CHEST] and continue. Defeat a few more Brownies and
turn at the fork, open the door, and loot the [CHEST]. Off in the alcove up the
path is another [CHEST] and a few more Brownies. Further north is a circular
area and in the corner are the last Brownies and a [CHEST].

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             Dangers of the Sidhe
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Arhaus Vorm
Location:    Vorm Lodge

  Speak with Arhaus who needs a rare plant, a Searstalk, to cure Luca Soren. Go
to the northern part of the Sidhe to find the item you seek. Return with the
[SEARSTALK] in hand for a lump of gold.

}}}

{{{
Quest Giver: Brit Codgan
Location:    Ysa

  Near the shops you can find Brit Codgan who wants your aid in reconstructing
a Faeblade. You can scour Ysa and loot the [FAE CACHES] until you have all the
parts required. Craft the [YSA HONOR BRAND] and return to Brit Codgan for about
500 gold; this quest is repeatable.
}}}

                                   Uprising
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Mythany Keen
Location:    Ysa - Embassy Hall

  Mythany Keen needs you to meet her in secrecy. In order to prevent an uprising
you are tasked with slaying Ambassador Brenner. Brenner will attempt to sway you
into deeling with Keen and now you can make the choice of who to side with. Kill
Brenner and loot the daggers then dispose of them, either by selling or
salvaging them at Blacksmith Forge. Report back to Ambasador Keen for a hefty
amount of gold and some rare ingredients and potions.
}}}

{{{
Quest Giver: Gertern Asker
Location:    Ysa - Asker's Alley

  Accept this quest and enter Lyceum Grove to find Jakasen. Test his potion and
you will wake up knowing the location of the Bristletongue, the Front. Grab the
weed then return to Gertern for a lump of gold.
}}}

                             Oh, the Indignitaries
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Squire Brio
Location:    Ysa

  Talk to Squire Brio to receive this quest. Seek out the four dignitaries and
question them about their ranks. Pay close attention and if you can, pass the
Persuasion Checks to get more background. Return to Squire Brio once you have
spoken with all the dignitaries and tell him the correct order:

- Great Huntress Hartwen
- Warlord Whenery
- Viscount Setter the Allseer
- Grand Faemage Gorrenet

  With the correct order you succeed and receive a chunk of gold. The wrong
order will fail the quest, so be sure to save.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

{{{
Quest Giver: Jorum Quintus
Location:    Ysa - Scholia Arcana

  Jorum suspects a few Initiates of thievery. Seek them out across the Sidhe
and loot their corpses for the journals: [ALOREN'S JOURNAL], [CASSERA'S JOURNAL]
and [BERTRAN'S JOURNAL]. Return to Jorum and inform him that:

- Cassera planned the theft.
- Bertran was murdered.
- Beasts killed Aloren.

  You receive the [MAGE'S GEM] and a sum of gold for your troubles.
}}}

Location:    Ysa - The Trellis

  Nomeron wants some help collecting water from each of the Sacred Pools. Seek
them out and open the Water Lock via the Flow Regulator in the Lyceum Grove.
Return to Nomeron to receive your reward, a random set of boots.

Quest Giver: Agraivin Hand
Location:    Star Camp
Requirement: Complete The Guided Hands

  Agraivin wants Prison Keys but the only way to get them is via Prison. Commit
some petty crime, such as stealing, in a major city and get caught. Request to
serve your time.

                                  Cureseeker
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Echostone
Location:    Ysa - Ballads Sanctuary

  Pick up [CURESEEKER] to the right of the Echostone then use the stone and
start the quest. The locations you need to go to and plant reagents are:

- Ayten, in the center square.
- Canneroc, in the center square.
- Didenhil, in the center near the well.
- Emaire, outside the Oddities and Curios.
- Gorhart, next to the inn.
- Mel Aglir, near the well.
- Tirin's Rest, across the northern bridge.
- Whitestone, in the corner of town.

}}}

Quest Giver: Sigra Thorin
Location:    Ayten - Thorin's Apothecary

  Sigra seems to have made some arithmetic errors on some invoices and needs you
to recollect them for her. Collect the invoices from the following:

- Iver House in Ayten.
- Hammer Smithy in Ayten
- The Golden Plains Inn at Ayten
- Nell's Items on the east side of Ayten
- Merchant Corpse to the west of Helmgard Keep.

  Return to Sigra Thorin who is quite pleased and gives you several potions as
your reward.
}}}

Quest Giver: Singing Nell
Location:    Ayten

  Go to the circle of Windstones in the southern half of the Wolds. Murghan and
a Banshaen wll attack you before you can activate them. Activate them in the
following order:

- Lowest
- Low
- Middle
- High
- Highest

  Return to Singing Nell to receive some gold and her disappointment.
}}}

Location:    Ayten
Requirement: Complete Ratofer's Pawns

  Approach Singing Nell and you can sell Ratofer's Ring for about 600 gold. You
can sell the Silverware to Banraun in the Smithy for about 75 Gold. Fynwick Iver
will buy the daggers for around 330 gold. Askel Thorin will purchase the
Kerchief for about 180 gold.

                             The Waters of Madness
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Alrette Rond
Location:    Rond Farm

  Alrette Rond has gone mad and cites the issues coming from the water. Go to
Cranalt and investigate. Kill the Cave Murghan at the entrance and loot the
corpse to find [JENNIKER'S JOURNAL]. Loot the [CHEST] and go south through the
toxic water. Check the western platform for a [LEVER] then continue south. Turn
west at the split and slay the Murghan guarding the [FAE CACHE]. Go south
through the water and fight the Cave Banshaen and Murghan. Loot the [FAE CACHE]
and the [CHEST] with the [MANA PENDULUM] inside.

  Go east and north for a moment to find a [FAE CACHE] in the eastern alcove.
Backtrack west through the door to find Murghan guarding the [CHEST] that holds
the [BELT OF FLUIDITY]. There is a [CHEST] to the south that is unmarked, but
you need to head to northern half now. Kill the Cave Murghan in the first room
to the north. Continue to the northern corner and loot the [FAE CACHE]. Enter
the water going west and take the southern path to a [FAE CACHE].

  Enter the southern room and use the [LEVER] then go to the northwest corner
and fight off another Banshaen. Loot the [CHEST] for the [GEM LATTICE] and go
to the far south to find a [FAE CACHE]. Return to the entrance room and repair
the artifact. Choose either Sanguine for optimism, Phlegmatic for reservedness,
or Melancholic for pessimism. Return to Alrette then back to Cranalt to turn off
the device and then back once more to Alrette to receive the reward.

}}}

                              A Pilgrim's Setback

 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Contract Board
Location:    Helmgard Keep

  Make your way to the northeast corner of the Forsaken Plain and into Mull-
Rane. Turn east and open the Hidden Door. Loot the [SKELETON] for [DULSTAN'S
NOTES] and the three [CHESTS]. Arcane Barghests strike as you open the
containers. Backtrack and go south to find a group of Kobold, one holds the
[SACRED TRACT]. Open the door and kill another Kobold for the second [SACRED
TRACT], then south for the third.

  Turn south and into the side room for a [CHEST]. At the southern end, two
more Kobolds, a [CHEST], and a [STONE OF AUTUMN]. Continue back north and open
the door then turn right to find another Hidden Door. This leads to two Kobold
and serves as a short cut back. Pay a visit to some Barghest in the southwest
then loot the [CHEST] they guarded. Turn around and go north to find the last
two Kobold that hold [SACRED TRACTS]. Open the northern door to find a [STONE OF
AUTUMN] then return to Helmgard.

}}}

{{{
Quest Giver: Contract Board
Location:    Helmgard Keep

  Enter the Lucky Mine in the northeast corner of west Kandrian. Check the two
[DIVE POINTS] and loot the [SKELETON] as you move north. Follow the fools then
turn east and fight the Freeman. Loot the two [CHESTS] and open the door. Turn
north and loot the [MINING CART] then follow the northern path west to two
[CHESTS]. Make your way back to the far east and kill the Freeman. Loot the
[CHEST] and go south to face Grinning Vane Spirrick. Loot his corpse for his
armband, search the southern area for a [CHEST] then claim the bounty.

Quest Giver: Heric Aster's Grave
Location:    South of Helmgard Keep along the eastern border

  Find this grave and take [HERIC'S AMULET] to receive [FINDING THE ASTER
INHERITANCE] and start the quest. In the southeast corner of Tala-Rane you can
find Bodan Aster's Grave to receive [BODAN'S AMULET] Head to the eastern border

the following locations:

- Southeastern corner in the Ettin camp.
- Final room in Dolve Wayle
- Against the western side of Dolve Wayle near a jump point.
- On a cliff at the southern junction of the Wolds.
- In the vault room of the Corgan Hold (northwest chambers).

{{{
Quest Giver: Niahm Kent
Location:    Along the road, east of Corgan Hold.

  You are tasked with slaying three Kobold leaders.

- Rotclaw can be found in the southwest corner in a small cave.
- Blackshriek is found along the river in the north along the eastern border.
- King Fan is found on the road to Kandrian.

  Return to Niahm once they are slain then seek out the Smiler, a Crudok, near
Corgan Hold. Return to Niahm and seek out the Ettin Warpriest Kolmir. Your last
task is to kill the Jottun Malgar in the south. Return to Niahm for you gold
reward.

{{{
Quest Giver: Faitir Scaith
Location:    West of Dolve Wayle

  Follow Faitir into Dolve Wayle. Loot the [CHEST] in the corner and head
south. Defend Faitir at the first stop then go east and kill The Scrivener.
Loot the [SCAITH FAMILY CURSE] and defend Faitir once more. Go east through
the rot and spike traps to find a [SKELETON] yielding the [CUIRASS OF N'GATAN].
Follow Faitir north and use the Shrine, on the backside of it is a moneybag.

  Go east and approach the First Scaith. You are obviously being led on by
Faitir but you have an option of siding with him or not.

Siding with the First Scaith
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Simply turn around and kill Faitir. The First Scaith releases the family of
the curse and you receive a hefty amount of gold and the [DOLVE WAYLE VAULT KEY]
that unlocks all the doors. With the key in hand, backtrack and open all the
doors that were previously locked to find a bunch of [CHESTS].

Siding with Faitir Scaith
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Kill the First Scaith, a strong summoner, and talk to Faitir. You receive a
bunch of gold and the [DOLVE WAYLE VAULT KEY]. Control over the Faer shifts to
Faitir and the quest concludes. With the key in hand, backtrack and open all the
doors that were previously locked to find a bunch of [CHESTS].

}}}

{{{
Quest Giver: Bardan Tam
Location:    Tam's Wagon

  Bardan Tam just wants his daughter back. Connovar has her hidden in Caer Tosai
to the south. Enter the dungeon and kill the first wave of enemies. Proceed east
and north past a few more rogues to find a [CHEST]. Take the alternate path
north to find more enemies and a [CHEST}. Go all the way west and down to reach
an area filled with crates and a [WEAPON RACK]. Backtrack to the center and take
the northern path this time and destroy the rogues here.

  Julia will emerge and talk with you, just send her back to her father and then
join her back at Tam's Wagon for your reward.

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Derfel's Labors
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Derfel
Location:    Derfel's House

  Speak with Derfel and he will want you to enter Lucky Mines and fine some
Rialte Brocaire. Simply enter the mines and go all the way north up the main
hallway to find a [CHEST] with the [RIALTE BROCAIRE] inside. Return to Derfel
for a staunch reward and your next task.

- You receive the [LETTER TO MATTIX DACE] and you need to deliver it to the man.
Venture over to Mel Aglir and find Mattix Dace in the Raven. Give him the letter
and return to Derfel for the next task.

- You need to find the corpse of Three Swords. Head to the northeast of east
Kandrian (technically Tywili Coast area) and find Three Swords. Loot his corpse
for [HELLBANE] and return to Derfel for another task.

- This time you are required to get three items. Start by heading south of
Derfel's to get the [ROSE OF KANDRIAN] from the grave of Jera Soren. Next, go to
Tirin's Rest and enter the Reedsong Inn. You can persuade Kells to sell the
[BLOODSTONE] for half price, otherwise it's about 3,000 gold. Lastly, go to
Rathir and enter the Scholia Arcana. In the Library is a [CHEST] with the
[THREADBARE CIRCLET] inside. This counts as three tasks when you return to
Derfel.

- Your seventh task is to forge the Amrynthian Band from the items you've been
collecting. Go north of Mel Aglir to Onarach. Speak with Hendi and watch how
fast she creates the band! Return to Derfel who needs help killing the man
who killed his wife. Head outside and aid him in battle. Afterwards, he tells
you of his secret fireplace and the treasures within. One of the [CHESTS] has
the [HELLBANE] you recovered earlier; the quest is complete.

}}}

{{{
Quest Giver: Eli Tems
Location:    Mel Aglir - The Raven

  Eli Tems wants the ring of the king. Head southeast to Kandrian Keep and make
your way to the King's chambers in the north. Open his dresser and loot the
[SIGNET RING OF LORD KANDRIAN] then return to Eli. The next task is to place
the ring on an altar in east Kandrian. Defend the ring from the Faer Gorta and
return to Eli once more. Return the ring to where you got it in the castle. You
have to take the back entrance through the cove.

  Sneak or fight your way into the King's chambers once more. Place the ring
and return to Eli for the final time. Your reward is a large amount of gold.

}}}

{{{
Quest Giver: Carasta Arawyn
Location:    Rathir - Officer's Hall

  You are tasked with coaxing Gwalchmai into an absurd deal using Maybryn Wine.
Give him a few bottles then Persuade him to sweeten the deal. Return to Carasta
for a healthy amount of gold.
}}}

                              A Second to a Duel
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Walen Forstid
Location:    Rathir - Seafoam Tavern

  Enter the Lower Tunnels and find Gelphyne. Buy the [ROSE-OF-SHADOWS] and go
to the Officer's Hall. Talk to Daltyn then apply the rose to the sword. Return
to Walen then leave the Inn. Walen's mother will approach and ask what's going
on. Lie or tell her the truth then see Jeibir, tell him either the Maid of
Fortune or The Ravenswing depending on what you want to happen.

  Go to the dueling ground and watch the scene then return to Jeibir or to
Walen's mother to collect your reward.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                   Bad Blood
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Onfei Cather
Location:    Rathir - Upper City

  Enter House Anwon and talk with Coriana. You need to obtain a Lapidus Root
that can only be found in Acatha. In the southern part of Acatha you can find
the [LAPIDUS ROOT] against the border. Use the Lapidus on Mallion to see him
restored then speak with Coriana. Head down to the Pryderi and talk with
Rhudlyn Rhewani in the Alchemist shop.

  Take her advice and see the City Watch to report the crime. Go to Abergast's
House and make Einar plead guilty. Loot his corpse for [DEATH'S VESTMENTS] then
return to Coriana with the news. She will give you [ORIEATOR'S SHIELD].
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                  The Orison
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Abelyra Seranon
Location:    Rathir - Temple of Lyria (Upper City)

  You are tasked with visiting three springs. There is one to the west of
Gloamthicket in Galafor. One in northern Galafor along the road to the Forsaken
Plain and one in the northern area of the Tywili Coast. Your second task is to
discredit Nuer in the Lower Tunnels who is preaching the word of Lyria wrong.
Generally choosing the bottom option gets the job done but you can always use
the persuasion checks to speed things along.

  Return to Abelyra and give up a max level gem, 10% of your levels experience,
or a percentage of your gold. The quest completes when you have given.
}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯

{{{
Quest Giver: Seila Twayn
Location:    Rathir - Temple of Lyria (Upper City)

  You are tasked with finding [RELICS] in Dolve Arne, Virki, Rithen, Kandrian, 
Dolve Wayle, and Corgan Hold. This task is repeatable and yields a hefty amount
of gold per turn in.
}}}

                                Learning Curve

 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Telemachus Rasp
Location:    Scholia Arcana Grounds

  Head to Gloamthicket in Acatha and slay the Cave Murghan as you move west
into a room. Go north from here to find more Murghan and a [CHEST]. Go west and
kill the Banshaen and a horde of Cave Murghan then loot the [CHEST] and return
to Telemachus for some gold.

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 A Page-Turner
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Idris Theonen
Location:    Scholia Arcana - Library

  Use the Omnibus Arcana in the grounds near the northern statue. Go to the
Rathir Bridge then read the book again. Head to Mel Aglir and read the book
once more. Go to Kandrian to the west of Tam's Wagon and fight off the ambush.
Read the tome again then return to the Scholia Arcana. Talk to Idris and answer
with "The Principle of Observation" to earn an extra 1000 gold.

}}}

                                    Galafor                           [07.13.00]

 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               Out of the Ruins
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Atheof Cergren
Location:    Tirin's Rest

  Atheof will start this quest and you can persuade him from the get go to
pay you up front! Head to Culn in the east part of the Tywili Coast and slay
the Tuatha before entering the Pengaras Basement. Speak with Bede then head to
Virki. Go straight from the entrance to a [CHEST] then take the western path.
Head into the rubble before the large room to find a [CHEST]. Help Anela with
the Tuatha then choose to go with her to close the gates.

  Search the [CHEST] and take the northwestern path. One side has a [CHEST]
free to loot, the other side also has a [CHEST] but is guarded by Faer Gorta.
Return to the central path and go northeast this time. Kill the Tuatha and
search the two [CHESTS]. Move to the next room where four Tuatha attack. There
is also a [CHEST] in the corner of this room. Enter the next room and kill the
Tuatha.

  Take the southern path, then stay south at the split to find two Tuatha and
a lever to close the first gate. Head north to find the same thing - two gates
down. Return to the central room and kill the Tuatha then go north and check
the alcove for a [CHEST]. At the northern end is the last of the Tuatha and
final lever to close the gate. Use the ladder in the central room for a quick
exit then return to Tirin's Rest. Speak to Atheof for some gold and the
[DOCTOR'S MEDALLION].
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Tirin's Secret
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Gwastl Brad
Location:    Tirin's Rest - Hwastle &amp; Cergren, Mercantile

  Talk with Gwastl and you can immediately see he's hiding something. Question
him about and the quest starts. Start asking around the town about a prisoner.
Florian Brennac in the Reedsong Inn will divulge some information about the
Burren Cove, so head on over there. You can take a shortcut through the backside
of the Sanctuary but for the purpose of collecting everything take the front
entrance.

  Persuade the guard to enter or take him out and break in. Take the eastern
path first to find a [CHEST] then take the southern path to find another. Kill
the Giant Rat to the south and loot the [CHEST] then talk to Adar. Head back to
Tirin's Rest and speak with Priestess Corelon, but she gives you nothing. Talk
to White Nil Kern and if you persuade him you can get [NIL KERNS' KEY]. If you
fail you must kill or steal from him to acquire it, the latter being the most
reasonable.

  Enter the Sanctuary and go upstairs to find a [SPELLBOOK] on how to release
Adar. Unlock the gate and break the circle to receive a [GEM OF GLOOM].
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                           The Valley of the Blessed
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Graem Haille
Location:    Tirin's Rest - Sanctuary

  Go to the northwest of Tirin's Rest to find Serabel Nareen. Talk to her to
discover she wants the Paling Wand from Adarus Hollow. Make the journey to the
cavern where Graem Haille will stop you and request you bring the Wand to her
instead. Enter the cavern and dispel the [CHEST] to your left. Go up the ramp
and slay the Sprites as you dispel another [CHEST]. Follow the path around to
some Boggarts and another [CHEST].

  Turn the corner into another room where more Sprites and a [CHEST] reside.
Further east you will encounter a Thresh and its Boggart companions. Slay the
creatures and loot the [CHEST] for the [PALING WAND]. Return the Paling wand
to Serabel for some herbs or give it to Graem for a chunk of gold and an
amulet.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Collections
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Meyra Maun
Location:    Tirin's Rest - Reedsong Inn

  Make a donation for the troops and then agree to take it to the Sanctuary for
Meyra. Deposit them and then wait around the Sanctuary till midnight to catch
Florian Brennac stealing. Report him to Corelon or let him go, neither choice
grants a reward.

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                          The Secret of the Fae Pools
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Kandir's Journal
Location:    Western border north of Gloamthicket

  This task requires some trial and error with the urns surrounding the stones.
Remove the Strange Red, Blue, and Purple stones from the urns. Use the diagram
below to achieve the desired results. Urn 1 is the northern-most urn.

        [1]      Poison Damage  - 1 = Red, 2 = Blue, 3 = Purple
                 No Effect      - 1 = Blue, 2 = Red, 3 = Purple
   [2]           Summon Boggart - 1 = Purple, 2 = Red, 3 = Blue
           [3]   No Effect      - 1 = Red, 2 = Purple, 3 = Blue
                 No Effect      - 1 = Purple, 2 = Blue, 3 = Red
                 Fire Damage    - 1 = Blue, 2 = Purple, 3 = Red

  The task never truly ends but at least you can conjure a Boggart.

}}}

                              They Walk Among Us
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Elrod Edman
Location:    South of Emaire

  Elrod suspects three of his men of spying for the Tuatha. Enter the Blue Bear
Tavern to find Anred Amfast. Persuade him to confess or kill him. Head to New
Culn in the southern part of east Forsaken Plains to find Froma Tonwald. Again,
persuade or kill and be on your way. At the Refugee Camp up north you can find
Nag Fendar. You have the option of Persuading him to confess or killing him.

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Unlucky Charm
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Wayne Emundas
Location:    Emaire - Blue Bear Tavern

  The robber has headed for the Cradle of Summer and can be found in the
northwest corner above Shardfall. Talk to Gelt Far to receive the [EYE OF
AMMAN] which immediately curses you with effects that can hurt you when you
attack! Go to Syl in the southeast and kill the Wolves in the first room. Loot
the two [CHESTS] and move to another room with Wolves. Check out the [CORPSE]
and the [CHEST] then go west to a room with two [CHESTS] and more Wolves.

  Return to the previous room and go north this time. There is a [CHEST] being
guarded by a Plant Snapper in the corner in this room. Go east and slay the
Sprites then check a [DIVE POINT] and two [CHESTS] before continuing. Jump down
and kill the Bog Thresh and Boggarts and loot two more [CHESTS]. Place the Eye
of Amman on the Ancient Altar and move through the Hidden Door. Return to Emaire
and give the Amulet to Edwin Hoswig for a few mediocre items or give it to
Wane Emundas for a bunch of gold and a ring.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                  Life's Work
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Odwald Bynothas
Location:    Emaire - Blue Bear Tavern

  Odwald is in search of a series of scholars notes. You can find them in the
following locations:

- Kallas' Notes are near the Windstone in northern Forsaken Plain.
- Dulstan's Notes are found in Mull-Rane during the quest A Pilgrim's Setback.
- Aewald's Notes are found in the Scholia Arcana Library in Rathir on the
  first bookshelf to the right.
- Wildfrod's Notes are found in the Luminary Leaf in Rathir on the first
  bookshelf to the right.

  Return to Odwald with all the notes to receive some Alchemy Recipes and a
minimal amount of gold.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             The Treasures of Culn
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Lord Cras
Location:    New Culn

  Enter Bitter Cove and disarm the trap in the first room to reach a [CHEST]
with the [TYRENIUM RING]. Down the hall is a [CHEST] and in the next room you
will find three Kobolds, a [CHEST], and the [PAINTING OF GALAFOR]. Kill the
Kobolds in the next room and loot the [CHEST]. Move towards another [CHEST] in
down the hall to have more Kobolds ambush you. Watch out for the trap and obtain
the [WINTER COURT NECKLACE].

  Disarm the tripwire in the next room to reach the [CHEST] containing the
[SUNSPAR BOX]. The final room has a large group of Kobolds, a [CHEST] with a
bear trap in front of it, and a [JADE URN] in the corner to complete the five
items. Return to Lord Cras and New Culn then follow his lacky quite a ways
north only to be tricked. You can convince him to stand down, otherwise you have
to kill him. Seek out Lord Cras on the docks in Rathir. You can either let him
go or put him in prison, letting him go results in some gold.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Buried Alive
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Ommer Vogard
Location:    Refugee Camp

  Enter Orieator's Tomb to the northwest and open the first [CHEST] on the
left to find the [SKILL BOOK (LOCKPICKING)]. There's another [CHEST] in the
corner and moneybag in the room as well. Use the Trap Lever to turn off the
blades in the hallway then progress to the next room. Talk with Lyra, loot the
[CHEST] and defend the group from the Faer Gorta that spawn. Return to Ommer for
a weapon as your reward.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               Raising the Dead
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Idwa Widfrond
Location:    Outside Orieator's Tomb

  You are in search of a particular grave, one that holds Azo Raemund's remains.
There is an [UNMARKED GRAVE] to the north of here, but it is not the one you
seek. Go to the southeast near Bitter Cove to find a letter in an [UNMARKED
GRAVE] then go to Emaire to find Britt Hagni. You can find him in Blue Bear
Tavern on the second floor. You have a few options so choose whichever you suits
you.

  You can walk away with [AZO'S WISDOM], [AZO'S WEALTH], and [AZO'S WISH] then
return to Idwa. Turn them or lie to her and keep them, the choice is yours.

}}}

                                Rivener Tarsus

 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Lord Callor
Location:    Deep Slumber

  You are tasked with finding parts of a broken Fae staff. Enter Mull-Rane and
fight to central area if you haven't been here before. Talk to Erion Raff and
purchase the Dark Sliver. Go to Emaire and into the Hagni Home to find The
God Fang. Go east of Emaire below the cliff and talk to Purta. If you cannot
persuade her to part with the Crack of Dawn you must kill her to get it.

  Go to Emaire and use the Blacksmith Forge behind the Blue Bear Tavern to craft
the staves. Break the staves down and rebuild them, then return to Lord Callor.
Ultimately, you get to keep the staves you made.

}}}

                                 Sisterly Love

Quest Giver: Lila Janick
Location:    Wandering near Deep Slumber

  You need to clear a way to the Sativa Fiber plants for Lila but spiders are
guarding it. Head over to the spiders and slay them, then return to Lila to
receive a discount on her wares.

{{{
Quest Giver: Terenia
Location:    Deep Slumber
Requirement: Complete The Great General

  After completing this quest you are often teleported to the Deep Slumber
where Terenia will confront you and start this quest. Protect her from the
Sprites, Trolls, Boggarts, and then Ancient Leanashe. You receive an amulet
for your hard work.

                              Worth Fighting For
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Hreid Amelthoe
Location:    Galette

  When accepting this quest you can persuade Hreid to give you more than half
of the turn out. Head down to the Galette Tunnels and fight with Hreid to clear
out the Kobolds. Loot the few [CHESTS] then return to the first room and talk
to Hreid. Go back to the second room and have Hreid inspect the corpse that is
infront of the glowing one. Then check the one just before you enter the dead
end.

  Return to the first room and open the door then defend Hreid from the
Testament. You will receive the [RING OF FYRAGBOS] and the [TOMB OF FYRAGNOS
KEY]. Enjoy the spoils behind the door you opened as the quest concludes.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             His Brother's Keeper
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Colm Alba
Location:    Galette

  This quest is best started after complete Worth Fighting For since you'll
get the [TOMB OF FYRAGNOS KEY]. Enter the tomb via the middle layer underneath
Galette. Follow Colm west through a pair of Giant Rats. Watch out for the
traps as you jump down to fight some Kobolds. Turn around the corner to find a
[CHEST] then continue to follow Colm. Kill the Testaments and a Niskaru then
check the [PILE] and move down the steps.

  Dodge the Fire Mines and turn off the course to a [CHEST]. Back on the main
path a little further, you can turn off again to a [PILE]. Slay the Kobolds at
the end and return to the Red Marches. Slay Giran before he can raise the
corpses then loot everything.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              Her Righteous Fury
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Eathe Dunbert
Location:    Galette
Requirement: Obtain the Tomb of Fyragnos Key

  Enter the Tomb of Fyragnos and follow Eathe north, using the [TOMB OF FYRAGNOS
KEY]. Search the eastern path for some Testaments and [PILE]. Go west and exit
the tomb to find a [STONE OF THE RED MARCHES] and a [CHEST]. At the fork go
west and fight off some Testaments to reach a [CHEST]. Go west when you can to
find more Testaments and a [CHEST] in the corner. Go south and then west at the
split to a ladder.

  Kill the Testaments out here and loot a [CHEST] and the [STONE OF THE RED
MARCHES]. Re-enter the Tomb of Fyragnos and return to where Eathe is located.
Take the southern exit to a [CHEST] then follow Eathe through the northern exit.
Kill the Testaments after Eathe poisons them to complete this section. Talk to
Eathe afterwards

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Into the Breach
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Colm Alba
Location:    Galette
Requirement: Complete Worth Fighting For, His Brother's Keeper, and
             Her Righteous Fury.

  This quests starts automatically once you've completed the requirement. Talk
to Colm Alba in Galette then enter the Tomb of Fyragnos. Go to the far south
and then east at the final split. Disarm the tripwire at the top of the steps
then enter the last room. Pick one of the members to stay behind, Hreid is the
weakest incase you needed aid choosing. Loot the [PILE] and the [CHEST] then
exit.

  Kill the Niskaru Bloodhunters first then focus on Fyragnos, a Niskaru Tyrant.
Every 25% Fyragnos will return to his fiery center and summon more Bloodhunters
for you to slay. Repeat this pattern until the beast is defeated. Dispel the
[CHEST] and talk to your allies to complete the quest.

}}}
================================================================================

                                   Alserund                           [07.17.00]
________________________________________________________________________________
================================================================================

 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                   Kidnapped
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Frama Aedic
Location:    Along the road north of Fellfire Pit

  Accept this quest and take the northern fork in the road from Frama heading
east. Talk to Florion in the Circle of Engard then head to the Caverns of
Ingress back west. Use the Erathi Sigil Stone near the waterfall and follow
the path. Clear the Boggarts and loot the [CHEST] then take the left path. Kill
a few more Boggarts and turn left once more to a second [CHEST]. Backtrack and
enter the middle area where an Ancient Leanashe and a [CHEST] reside.

  Make your way north to a [CHEST] and a group of Brownies and a Crudok. Go all
the way south after hitting this Erathi Sigil Stone to find the tree. Use this
last Erathi Sigil Stone and meet the Thresh to the east. Loot the corpse for the
[KORA PETAL] then return to Lorion. Use the potion on the Almain and the quest
is complete.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Fellfire Bloom
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Florion
Location:    Circle of Engard
Requirement: Complete Kidnapped

  Head to the Fellfire Pit and follow the western path. Kill the Sprites and
continue down the path. Clear out the Kobolds and loot the [CHESTS]. As you move
north use the Altar of Belen and slay the Niskaru Tyrant. Loot the [FELLFIRE
BLOOM] and go north to a Hidden Door where you can find a [CHEST]. Continue east
and kill some Sprites to reach another [CHEST]. Further along are some Kobolds
and a [CHEST] then a spot to jump down and exit. Return to Florion to complete
the quest.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 The Crossing
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Florion
Location:    Circle of Engard
Requirement: Complete Fellfire Bloom

  Head to the western side of Alserund and challenge Pura. After you win the
duel you receive the [AMULET OF THE SUN]. Go south to Caer Elatha and turn west
to a [CHEST] once inside. Go east and then south to a [CHEST] then talk to Maxen
to be granted access. Continue east and turn north to find a Leanashe and a
[CHEST]. Go south and fight off the Sprites then loot the [CHEST] before
resuming.

  Defeat the Boggarts to reach the [CHEST] then turn east to find Barghests. Go
north and slay the Troll, look west for a [CHEST], and go east to continue.
Dismantle the Boggarts in the hall and look north for a [CHEST]. Head south into
the water where you'll find numerous [DIVE POINTS] and [FAE CACHES]. Continue
east through the water to find many of the same treasures as the previous room.
Approach Halcyor, who is a little crazy, then defeat him.

  Place the Fellfire Bloom atop the altar then return to Maxen to receive the
[WHISPERSKIN SANDALS], a great set of caster boots. Return to Florion in the
Circle of Engard

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Fae at the Mine
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Apule Vire
Location:    Motus Mining Outpost

  Find Enser and lead the way towards the Fae. Kill the Boggarts and then the
Sprites and turn the corner to find more Sprites. Speak with Aurenda and then
Enser. Jump down and go west to find a corpse with [AURENDA'S LIGHT] then enter
Shadowthorn. Turn left at the intersection and fight off the Sprites so you can
reach the [CHEST]. Return to the central path and go right this time to find
some Boggarts and another [CHEST].

  Back to the main path you are forced west where Barghests lurk. Grab the
[CHEST] near the rooms entrance and go west to a [CHEST] perched on a platform.
Go all the way north and dispel the [CHEST] then continue east. Dispel the door
and defeat the Leanashe then talk to Aurenda to receive the a random necklace.
Loot the [CHEST] on your way out then seek out Enser at the Outpost for your
reward.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                   Bloodbane
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Capstan Odvar
Location:    Motus Mining Outpost

  Talk to Edgar to west and he will mark a location of Brownies that will
surely draw the Crudok out.
}}}

                              The Century Flowers
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Calovar
Location:    Motus Mining Outpost

  You receive some [PETRICHOR] and are on your way. Seek out the three Flowers
and use fire on them then you activate the Flower to force it to bloom. Return
to Calovar once they are all bloomed

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              Miners in the Sand
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Apule Vire
Location:    Motus Mining Outpost
Requirement: Complete Bloodbane

  Speak with Calovar then head west to find Edgar Aron. Enter the Aron Mine
and convince Edgar to part with the stone by any means. Seek out the miners and
talk to them with the stone in hand to release them from the spell. Return to
Apule once all five have been cured for your reward and access to Edgar's old
facility. Return the Relic to Calovar to finish the quest.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               Aron Excavations
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Calover
Location:    Motus Mining Outpost
Requirement: Complete Miners in the Sand

  This quest starts immediately after completing Miners in the Sand. To finish
this task simply purchase all the upgrades. When fully upgraded, you'll have
access to a plethora of loot including the [SKILL BOOK (MERCANTILE)] on a
bookshelf on the second floor.

}}}

[ELDRIC'S STAFF] and collect the bounty.

                                 Spider Season
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Contract Board
Location:    Ironfast Keep

  Seek out the spiders around Menetyre and loot them for the [SPIDER STINGERS]
they drop. Return to collect the bounty once you've acquired eight of them.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               A Master's Touch
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Gavroche Valle
Location:    Ironfast Keep

  Head to the southern part of Menetyre and follow the path around to a high
platform where you will find the Hermit. Speak with him to realize he is in
need of aid. Persuade him to go to Ironfast and he will start the quest Time of
Need. After healing Efyr seek out the [MASTER'S TARROW]. You can find some in
the Tearscotter Mine or from Hurvar's Doorsill. With the item in hand, return
to Efyr in Ironfast Keep. Watch the Hermit Smith craft [HALDEBIER'S BLADE] and
receive it as a gift as the quest concludes.

Note: If you didn't venture into Hurvar's Doorsill it's quite the adventure and
      has plenty of loot and Niskaru to fight.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Time of Need
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Efyr Dynnwel
Location:    South central Menetyre

  Slay a few spiders to acquire the [SPIDERSAC ICHOR]. Head north of the Hermit
to find [FENNWRAC FLOWER] in the canyon. Reach the upper levels of the zone
where you'll find plenty of Jottun and the grist required. Return to Efyr and
he will be cured.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Making Enemies
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Orsinian Paige
Location:    South of Hurvar's Doorsil

  Go to the southeastern corner of Menetyre to find the Tearscotter Mine,
currently guarded by Kobolds. Slay the Kobolds in the first room and loot the
[CHEST] to the south. Head north to find more Kobold willing to die then go
through the doorway to find two [CHESTS]. Stay north and open the door as you
stumble upon another [CHEST]. Go west at the end to find the last of the
Kobold then steal the [KOBOLD CLAN TOTEM].

  Loot the three [CHESTS] and go down the other path though the water. The
[CHEST] here has the [MOTUS REPORTS IV]. Check the [DIVE POINTS] and continue
south to find Giant Rats. Go east then south to another [CHEST], this one holds
the [MOTUS MINING SURVEY]. Continue to the west to find some Kobolds, a [CHEST],
and a [MINING CART] worth looting. Leave the area and return to Orsinian Paige.
You're next task is to slay some Jottun and plant the Kobold daggers on their
corpses.

  Head to the heights and kill the Chosen, planting the daggers as you go. Meet
Orsinian near the Hermit's camp and watch the battle unfold. When one side has
been the victor jump down and finish the rest. Talk to Orsinian to finish the
quest and receive a handsome reward.

}}}
