¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             Whitestone Tarnished
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Motus Mining (Day x)
Location:    Several

  You can find the Motus Mining notes around Menetyre. The one you likely have
acquired first is Day 51 while crossing into Apotyre from Menetyre.

- Motus Mining (Days 1-24) is found in a chest on the second floor of the
  Thirsty Wench in Whitestone.
- Motus Mining (Days 25-44) is found on an unmarked Bookshelf on the platforms
  in the Sun Camp.
- Motus Mining (Days 45-50) is found in a Dresser south of Snaketail Grotto
- Motus Mining (Day 51) is found on a corpse on the junction of Menetyre and
  Apotyre.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                   Bone Town
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Beorn
Location:    Whitestone

  Greet Beorn at the entrance to Whitestone. He's pretty adamant about you
meeting the Mayor so head on over to the Mayor's House. Talk to the Mayor and
agree to help him out. You can also use the Hidden Door aka his fireplace to
reveal a [CHEST] and a [PILE]. You can also steal the [KEY TO MAYOR'S CAVE]
from the Armoire up the stairs, it will come in handy. Head over to the Motus
Mining Headquarters and search the Bookshelf for the [DEED TO SKORIA MINE].

  Return to the Mayor with the deed then head to the Cynric Quarry. Follow the
path west killing the Cynrics as you happen upon a [CHEST] in the corner. Go
north to three more Cynrics and another [CHEST]. Continue north to find Adath
Skoria. He explains himself and then leaves. Open the [CHEST] nearby and head
east to a [MINING CART] with a [CULMINITE DEPOSIT] inside then head north to
the final [CHEST]. Cynrics attack you from behind, kill them to complete a
secondary task, The Cynrics.

  Speak with the Mayor of Whitestone and then make a decision to work with or
without him.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Opening a Vein
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Mayor Eswin Ealfhelm
Location:    Whitestone

  This quest has two paths based on whether or not you sided with the Mayor.

Siding with the Mayor
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Head to Skoria Mine and loot the [CHEST] in the entrance room. Persuade or
pay Thelgood Skoria to let you pass and go east to find Niskaru. Loot the
[CHEST] and go south where you can find another. Go north and kill two more
Niskaru then turn west to find five more. Loot the two [CHESTS] as you move
south past a pair of corpses. Defeat the Niskaru Tyrant and search for two
[CHESTS] and a [MINING CART].

  Go all the way south to another [CHEST] then turn east for another [CHEST] and
a [MINING CART] with the [ORE SAMPLE]. Exit the mine and return to the Mayor.
The final task is to slay Adath Skoria. Loot the [SKORIA FAMILY RING] and return
to the Mayor for your reward.

Siding with the Adath Skoria
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Talk with Adath to receive the [SKORIA FAMILY RING] then head to the Skoria
Mine. Loot the [CHEST] in the entrance room and show the ring to Thelgood so
you can pass and go east to find Niskaru. Loot the [CHEST] and go south where
you can find another. Go north and kill two more Niskaru then turn west to find
five more. Loot the two [CHESTS] as you move south past a pair of corpses.
Defeat the Niskaru Tyrant and search for two [CHESTS] and a [MINING CART].

  Go all the way south to another [CHEST] then turn east for another [CHEST] and
a [MINING CART] with the [ORE SAMPLE]. Exit the mine and return to Adath. He
wants you to kill the Mayor to end this once and for all. You can either kill
him or persuade him to go to jail. Speak with Adath for your reward and the
quest ends.
}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                   Runaways
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Steg Darkvari
Location:    Whitestone

  Steal the key to the [WHITESTONE CAGE KEY] from Beorn and release Steg. Head
to the Darkvari Mine and kill the first wave of Outlaws. Search the Whirlpool
then head west, just watch out for the trap. Turn the corner and kill two more
Outlaws then go south to a [CHEST] and further to Giant Rats and a footlocker
containing a [CULMINITE DEPOSIT]. Go back east and kill the last Darkvari then
loot [STEG DARKVARI'S TRUNK] at the end of the path for the [MYSTERIOUS
PARCHMENT].

  Outside you will encounter Hrindi Zungar. Either give her the parchment, kill
her, or convince her that it's a bad idea. Return to Steg near the Skoria Mine
and tell him whatever you want. As long as you kept the parchment it will turn
into the [DARKVARI TREASURE MAP] as the quest completes. Use the item to mark
locations of interest on your map.
}}}

{{{
Quest Giver: The Bone Wall

reward.

gold if you want, otherwise you don't get a reward.

  You are to deliver notices of death. Head outside and talk to Vonne Gortan,

to inform Edwin of his brother's death. Once you've made it to Mel Senshir you
can find Fridi Edstar to give her the bad news. Return to Squire Coran when all
the notices have been passed out for your reward.

out Scholar Airancourt in the Basilica Gnostra. After the confession return to
Courdan with the news.

{{{
Quest Giver: Feride Ouet
Location:    Adessa - Laboratories

  Enter Adessa Mine and loot the [CHEST] in the initial room. Speak with Feride
in the next room to start the experiment. Kill the Brownies, Boggarts, Kobold,
and finally the Troll. You receive several potions and a large quantity of gold
for your efforts, but you might as well explore the rest of the Mine while
you're here.

  Go east through the door the loot the [MINING CART] the further to some Giant
Rats. Slay them and search the moneybag as you go south. Disarm the tripwire
and slay the Kobolds then loot the [CHEST] and [WEAPON RACK] to complete the
mine.

                                  Paper Trail
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Chapter I: Preliminary Plans
Location:    Adessa - The Livrarium

  Find this book on a table in the Livrarium. You receive [ADESSA I] to start
but you need to find the second book. Head to the Praetorian Garrison to find
[ADESSA II] on a bookshelf near the Sparring Arena. Head into Laboratories next
and go to the top floor to find [ADESSA III] on a bookshelf. Next up is the
Domus Politica where [ADESSA IV] rests on a bookshelf in the upper floors. You
can find [ADESSA V] in the Grand Bursars along the northern wal.

  Go to the Arcadium and search the bookshelf in the back for [ADESSA VI]. Head
through the Isles and into the Basilica Gnostra where [ADESSA VII] can be found.
Search the Forum for [ADESSA VIII] then return to the Livrarium and search the
bookshelf in the back corner to find the [BOOK OF PERSUASION].

}}}

                                 Eyes and Ears
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Captain Drefan
Location:    Outside Mel Senshir

  You need to find the three Scouts that the Captain sent out. One can be found
north of Seven Widow Mine in the southeast. A second scout can be found east of
Shattertier Mine in the north of Cursewood. The third scout is in the Midden
southwest of the Proving Halls. Return to Captain Drefan for some gold once
you've located all three scouts.
}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                    Deadeye
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Elias Hurk
Location:    Outside Shattertier Mine

  Elias won't return to Captain Drefan unless he kills Deadeye. That's where you
come in handy! Enter the mine and check the [DIVE POINT] at the entrance. Head
north and kill the Bolgan then continue east to find some Brownies. Go west and
break the crates to reach a [CHEST] then go north. Kill the two Bolgan and loot
the two [CHESTS] before going west to fight Deadeye. Kill Deadeye and loot the
[CHESTS] on your way back to Elias.

}}}

Quest Giver: Malthon
Location:    House of Sorrows

  Burn the corpses around the Midden to lure out Meathgra. Enter her den and
kill the Leanashe (and her Brownies). Search the side rooms for a few more
foes and a [CHEST] then return to Malthon to receive a [PARAMOUNT GEM].

{{{
Quest Giver: Betheli Jons
Location:    Camp south of the Proving Halls

  Make the Headsman go away and Betheli will rush at you and request you chase
him down and kill him. Head to Tinehil and speak with the Headsman then loot
the [CHEST]. Go to the northwest and slay the Brownies and loot a [CHEST[, Move
southeast to a group of Boggarts and a [FAE CACHE] tucked away in the corner.
Go north into the water and search the [DIVE POINT] before finding the [CHEST]
in the alcove.

  Make your way north and open the door to find Sprites guarding a [FAE CACHE].
Dispel the [CHEST] in the next room before meeting the Headsman. Kill him and
loot the [FAE CACHE]. Move south to a warded [CHEST] then use the jump point for
a quick out-route back to Betheli. Your reward is a chunk of gold.

Note: There is a Hidden Door south of here with a [CHEST] that holds the [ROBE
      OF SEASONS].

}}}

Quest Giver: Sinon Carrag
Location:    Alfar Camp

  Seek out the Banshaen to the west in their little watery corners. The last one
is to the far south past the Sanctuary Grotto. You can take a small passage
that leads to Tinniat's Burial Cairn to receive [TINNIAT'S HAUBERK].

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             Artifacts and Castles
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Ariel Perien
Location:    East of Bonnlach

  Just north of Ariel you can find Deod Dungaras' corpse with [ARIEL'S PACK] on
it. Return the pack to Ariel near Bonnlach then head inside the castle. Go east
through the watery hallway to find Murghan and a Banshaen. Loot the [CHEST] and
proceed south up the staircase. As you move east take a pitstop south and break
the urns to find a [CHEST]. Continue east down into a watery area once more
where a Banshaen will disrupt your exploring.

  Search behind the throne for a warded [CHEST] then take the left path going
north to a Hidden Door. Kill the Murghan and loot the [CHEST] and open the door
making sure to avoid the spike trap. Move through the hall to find two [CHESTS],
one guarded by Murghan. Return to the throne room and take the other path going
north to find a [CHEST] before the stairs. Turn the corner going east and slay
the Murghan then proceed through the door to a room full of traps.

  Open the [CHEST] in the back then return to the previous hallway and unlock
the next door to reach another [CHEST]. Move to the southeast corner to find the
[ANCIENT ARTIFACT] in the [CHEST]. Talk to Ariel to receive some gold and the
quest ends.

}}}

                           Witch Knight of Ghenning
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Audra Firan
Location:    Camp south of Ghenning

  Head north of Audra and kill the Jottun Runelord to find the [CAGE KEY].
Dispel the [CHEST] while you're here then return to Audra. Follow her up to
Ghennig then go down the central path. All the way down the steps you will find
three Jottun and a [CHEST] in the corner. Continue north and kill more Jottun
then loot the [CHEST]. Clear out the Jottun in the final room to the north then
make your way back to the entrance room.

  Take the southern path this time and fight through the Jottun up the stairs
where a [CHEST] lies. Go through the door and slay more Jottun as you ascend
the staircase. Slay Khleran and the Jottun in this last room and loot the [DEMON
HORNS] and [KHLERAN'S SCEPTRE] from his corpse. Search the [CHEST] in the corner
then take your leave.

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               True to the Cycle
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Liordran
Location:    Northwest corner off the road

  You receive [ALLEIA'S RING] from Liordran, now you need to take it south.
Follow the road until you reach Rahnil where you will find two [CHESTS] in the
first room. Move west where you'll encounter a Bog Thresh and a few Sprites.
Snag the contents of the [CHEST] then proceed west to another Bog Thresh and
some Boggarts. Follow the path around the curve with a [CHEST] along the way to
more Boggarts and another [CHEST]. Kill the Sprites in the final room and place
Alleia's Ring on the altar.

  Take the other path back where you will encounter Arcane Barghest and a warded
[CHEST]. Jump down to make for a fast exit and return to Liordran.

}}}

                                 Brun the Bard
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Brun the Bard
Location:    Odi's Camp

  Speak with Brun then move across the nearby bridge and kill the Bolgan. Hear
the story Brun has to tell then move to the Castle Gastyr and slay the Bolgan
here. Loot the area as you wait for Brun then listen to the story. Move west and
clear the cliffs to hear Brun's final story. Enter the Castle Gastyr in search
of Brun's letter.

  Move south into the first room and defeat the Arcane Barghest that strike.
Check the [CHEST] and a second one to the south. Move east to find Hillared
Gastyr and start another quest. Follow Hillared and refer to The Last Gastyr
quest. Once you have the letter return to Brun in Odi's Camp for your reward.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                The Last Gastyr
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Hillared Gastyr
Location:    Castle Gastyr

  Follow Hillared east and loot the [CHEST] in the corner to find [TO LORD
GASTYR 1], then defeat the enemies. In the next room you will find a [CHEST] at
the entrance and a pair of Bolgan. Fight off the Bolgan as more will surely come
down the steps. Proceed up the stairs and turn north to find a locked [CHEST].
In the other corner you can find a Prismere Troll guarding a second [CHEST].
Unlock the southern door if you wish to fight another Troll and check the final
corner of the room for the third [CHEST].

  Move west up the stairs and cleanse the room of Bolgan and Barghest. Empty the
two [CHESTS] and proceed through the hallways. As you enter another room check
the [CHEST] to find [TO LORD GASTYR 2] then move south and clear the area. Open
the northeast gate to find a [CHEST] behind all the crates. Go south to the dead
end room and clear it then empty the two [CHESTS]. Make your way east up the
stairs and into another room with Bolgan. Kill them and loot the [CHEST] to get
[TO LORD GASTYR 3] then proceed to the final room.

  Kill the Ancient Leanashe first then focus on Racinon. Talk to Hillared to
receive [RIGHTEOUS] and loot the two [CHESTS]. For Brun the Bard, loot [LORD
GASTYR'S CHEST] to receive the [LETTER FORM LORD ERRAN GASTYR].

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              Worthy of Chernobog
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Aloff the Hunter
Location:    East of Odi's Camp

  After Aloff's speech seek out Bolgan and collect 10 [BOLGAN EYES]. When you
have at least 10 eyes enter the cave to the east of Aloff's camp. Light the
offering and slay Chernobog to receive the [HELM OF BOLGANS' BANE] and
[CHERNOBOG'S EYE].

Note: Just south of Aloff you can find a Hidden Door that leads to a [CHEST]
      containing the [TUATHA COWL].

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              The Lady's Children
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Private Janara
Location:    Ansilla's Camp

  You are tasked with recovering five of Lady Ansilla's dolls:

- Inside Seawatch on the southern end in a fallen Shelf.
- North of the camp inside a log where a Skeleton holds the doll.
- Inside a chest in Castle Ansilla in the room where you raise the portcullis.
- In the room where you fight Ticneri, in a chest.
- Carried by a Tuatha Soldier at the front gate of Castle Ansilla.

  Return to Private Janara with all the dolls to receive some armor and gold.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                            The Blades and the Seal
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Drewn Ansilla
Location:    Ansilla's Camp

  Head to Castle Gastyr to find Hillared Gastyr. Complete her quest and ask
aboout Drewn, then the Ansilla Key. Persuade her and she hands over the [THE
ANSILLA KEY]. Head to Seawatch and kill the Bolgan in the first room. Empty the
[CHESTS] and move south to find the [ANSILLA FAMILY LOCK BOX] with the [ROYAL
SEAL OF ANSILLA] inside. Return to Drewn with the seal and he lets you keep
the blades as a reward.

NOTE! - Once you have turned the key back in you will never be able to retrieve
        it. There are additional lock boxes in the Shadow Labyrinth in the
        Forsaken Plains, in Seawatch, and in the Castle Ansilla. Only return the
        key once you have opened these lock boxes.


}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                The Lost Squad
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: General Fynn
Location:    Northwest of Castle Ansilla

  Enter the nearby pipe and loot the [CHEST] then go south killing a pair of
Tuatha.  Kill the Tuatha in the next room and check the [CHEST] for [TO LADY
ANSILLA 1]. Ahead you'll find a group of Zealots, Conni, and a [CHEST]. The next
room houses Ridge Gautliffe who doesn't seem to threatened by the Tuatha. Follow
him to the main foyer then go southeast to find a Tuatha Priest and a [CHEST].
The next room has a few more Tuatha and [CHEST] containing the [ANSILLA DUNGEON
KEY].

  Return to the foyer and follow Ridge to the next room. Clear this place out
and check the [CHEST] as you move south. Use the lever and move into the final
room where Ticneri and a large group of Tuatha are located. As Ticneri falls
you are afflicted with a Soulbind Curse. Loot the [CHESTS] to find [TO LADY
ANSILLA 2] then go back down to the alchemy lab. Dispel the [CHEST] and use the
[MYSTERIOUS CURE] found inside. Return to General Fynn to receive [CRYSTALLINE
BARRIER] as your reward.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              Ghosts of Seawatch
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Byrn Elgar
Location:    Seawatch

  Talk to Byrn to discover the castle of Seawatch is now yours. He suggests you
get to bringing back the rest of the staff, starting with Conni. Search the
northern portion of the castle for some [PILES] and [SKELETONS] then go to the
Castle Ansilla. If you enter the pipe during the quest The Lost Squad you can
find Conni in the first major room. Refer to The Lost Squad until you have the
key then release Conni. Go back to Seawatch and speak with Byrn to get details
on the next person.

  Note the upgrades to the keep, it is recommended that you raid the containers
at this point. Head to Odi's Camp and the Sergeant is more then willing to leave
but wants a replacement first. Seek out Private Cornall to the southwest and
convince him to replace the Sergeant. Return to Odi who heads off to Seawatch.
Speak with Byrn and raid the castle once more then head back to Mel Senshir.
Talk to Astor Colliani then enter the tavern.

  Talk to Fridi and either persuade her to give you the dagger or purchase it
from her. Return to Astor and he will head back to Seawatch. Talk to Byrn to
complete the quest and receive the final upgrade to the keep.

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             The Siege of Moondown
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Captain Canwen
Location:    Camp Moondown

  Talk to Captain Canwen and half sentence she is cut off as Tuatha strike the
camp. After the battle talk to the Captain and agree to find the camps Healer,
Colm. Head to Glasspillar Caves and slay the Tuatha and Bolgan in the first
room. Loot the [WEAPON RACK] and turn north to find a [CHEST]. In the next
room kill the Tuatha Bolgan Master then empty the [CHEST]. Follow the path to
another [CHEST] and a singular Bolgan in a room.

  Move south along the path, killing the Tuatha that impede your progress. Turn
east and empty the [CHEST] then defeat the remaining Tuatha. Loot the [CHEST] in
the corner and talk to Colm. Provide him a Master Healing Potion then escort him
out. Kill the Bolgan and loot a [CHEST] and [COLM'S PACK] on your way back to
the Camp. Talk to the Captain then go to the Whispering Caves in search of the
Weaponsmith.

  Enter the cave and eliminate the Faer Gorta that strike. Go east then north
to a [CHEST] then jump down. Move south to a [DIVE POINT] then slay the few
Faer Gorta that attack you. Pull the lever and talk to Anella Saff who is a
little displeased with you. Check the [CHEST] to the south and then another
next to a [WHIRLPOOL] further down. Follow her around the corner and slay the
Tuatha then pluck the [BREATH OF ARBA] from the statue. Protect Anella from the
Faer then escort her out.

  Take a turn to the north and slay the Tuatha that guard a [CHEST] then you
may continue west. Loot the [CHEST] in the hallway then kill the enemies that
ambush you. Disarm the tripwire trap to the north and grab the final [CHEST] as
you make your way back to the camp. Defend the camp once more then head to the
bridge and speak with Gorem Kane. Pay or persuade the man to help or burn the
towers for him.

  You receive the [TORCH] you need to light towers, all that's left to do is
destroy the camps enemies and light the towers on fire. With the mercenaries
back in Camp Moondown you must give a speech. There are several speech checks,
passing them all results in boosted morale for the final battle at the camp.

}}}

                                  Bolgan Bane
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Knave of Pride
Location:    Camp Moondown

  Hunt down the Tuatha Bolgan Masters around the area. Start to the south of
camp then follow the main road to reach the second Master. The last group can be
found inside Glasspillar Caves. Return to the Knave of Pride once the Bolgan
Masters have been slain for your reward.

                              The Killing Ground
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Desiderus Trav
Location:    Ariad Camp

  Move south and up the ridge then slay the Tuatha Priest. Loot the [CHEST] and
jump down to talk with Desiderus Trav. Move further south and up the next ramp
to a Tuatha Priest. Dispel the [CHEST] and move across the bridge to the last
Tuatha Priest. Dispel this [CHEST] and jump down, returning to Desiderus. Follow
his lead and slay the Tuatha and Prismere Troll ahead. Follow Desiderus to the
final camp where the Witch Knight Dessidyn is located. Slay the leader and
Desiderus will set up camp in this new location.

}}}

                                     Gask
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Aluck
Location:    Ashmoor

  Fight your way to the far east past the Echoing Light Mine and kill the Witch
Knight near the Sagecraft Altar. Make your way north from here and slay the
second Witch Knight. Go south to find Gask and the last of the Tuatha in this
zone. Eradicate them and speak with Aluck to receive no reward.

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                     Esha
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Esha
Location:    Glowlode Mine

  Find Esha in the Glowlode Mine and escort her and the Ashmoor Survivors to
the north. Loot the [SKELETON] on your way to the Cave Murghan. There is a
[WHIRLPOOL] in the next room filled with Murghan and another along the way to a
Banshaen. Slay the beast and check the [SKELETON] then go north at the fork to
find a [CHEST] and another [WHIRLPOOL]. Step into Shadow Pass to complete the
quest then go back in and search the southern part of the previous fork to find
a [WHIRLPOOL] and a Bolgan guarding two [CHESTS].

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                     Ordo
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Ordo
Location:    Weconai

  Enter Weconai and use the Erathi Sigil-Stone to release Ordo. Agree to help
him find the Fateweaver then open the Hidden Door to find three [CHESTS]. Move
south into the next room and slay the two Banshaen. Loot the [CHEST] and go
south where you can jump down to find a [STONE OF AUTUMN]. Follow the path to an
open area with Cave Murghan abound. Dispel the [CHEST] as you move west to a
door. Protect Ordo at this point until the door is opened then proceed.

  Up the stairs you will find a few Murghan and a [WHIRLPOOL] just before the
next door. Continue up the steps to find four [CHESTS] and Maura. Speak with her
then either slay her or let her take Ordo. To the east you will find another
[STONE OF AUTUMN] and the quest should have ended with either result.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                    Bareth
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Nel
Location:    Echoing Light Mine

  Release Nel then agree to help her. Go north at the split and kill the Tuatha
as you enter a room with a [CHEST]. Go south to find more Tuatha and check
Bareth's Corpse. Continue south and check the [GLITTERING PILE] to find a
[MURGHAN CHARM]. Kill the Tuatha in this room and loot the treasures before
going east. Defeat Cryamor and the Tuatha then return to Nel to receive the
[ERATHI GLYPH]. Use the glyph to open the [EVENTIDE TREASURE] in Eventide.

}}}

                                    Amaura                            [07.29.00]

 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Master Belne
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Master Belne
Location:    Cann-Rane

  Enter Cann-Rane and slay the Tuatha as you move to the second room. Check the
Hidden Door for a [CHEST] then speak with Master Belne. Use your Blacksmithing
skill to convince Belne to craft something for you then accept his quest. Loot
the [WEAPON RACKS] and head up the stairs to a [CHEST] then slay the Tuatha
Overlords, looting their corpses for the components. Return to Master Belne and
choose the item you wish to create.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               Master Farraglen
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Master Farraglen
Location:    Cann-Rane
Requirement: Complete Master Belne

  Up the steps from Master Belne are two [CHESTS] and Master Farraglen. Accept
the quest and follow the path to two Tuatha and a [CHEST] containing the first
[PREPARED RAW PRISMERE]. Go north to find a [CHEST] then double back and go
south. Empty the [CHEST] in this small room to acquire the second [PREPARED RAW
PRISMERE]. From the central room take the final path east where two Tuatha will
charge you. Kill them then loot the [CHEST] for the final [PREPARED RAW
PRISMERE]. Open the door and talk to Master Farraglen to receive [FARRAGLEN'S
GEM].

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Master Kiftal
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Master Kiftal
Location:    Cann-Rane
Requirement: Complete Master Farraglen

  For this task you must go out into Amaura. Jump down into the water and snag
the [SORROGWETH FUNGUS] then return to Kiftal. You receive [KIFTAL'S ELIXER] as
the quest is complete.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             Heroes Shall Not Pass
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Master Kiftal
Location:    Cann-Rane
Requirement: Complete Master Kiftal

  Head to the barrier and disable it then kill Witch Knight Anira. Return to
Kiftal to receive [NEARTH'S HAMMER] and a few potions and gold. Search the
area east of Anira to find several Faer Gorta and a bunch of [CHESTS]. You can
also find a Hidden Door before the jump point near the entrance where another
[CHEST] resides.
}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               The Commendation
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Ost Ordura
Location:    Gorhart - Inn

  You are tasked with slaying the Krast brothers. Osgar Krast can be found in
the west half of Odarath at the northern camp. Medgar Krast can be found in the
east half of Odarath in the northern camp. Slay them both and return to Ost
Ordura to complete the quest and take another towards becoming part of the
Warsworn.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                The Road Patrol
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Ost Ordura
Location:    Gorhart - Inn
Requirement: Complete The Commendation

  Seek out Castellan Tine Delfric in Shieldring Keep. Head to the southern part
of east Odarath to find the Keep. You receive your first mission from Tine and
you need to reach Didenhil. Search the southwestern hall for a [CHEST] that
won't require you to steal, a [WEAPON RACK], and the services that are provided.
Enter the Healer's Cottage in Didenhil and speak with Wyl Rendig then head east
into Lorca-Rane.

  Begin searching the clues that are along the path east. Crand is the lucky
victim as you come across the last clue. Regroup with Ost then scour the area
for more clues. Another person is slain as you find the last clue again.
After grouping up again, approach the wagon to spawn a Niskaru Bloodhunter. If
this is your first time facing this creature be prepared for what could be a
difficult dual. Alone, the Niskaru aren't as challenging but in groups they can
be devastating.

  As Ost pays his respects, loot the cart and the [CHEST] then follow him as
you head after the Niskaru. Enter Brigand Hall Caverns as [THE HEART OF SIBUN]
begins.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              The Heart of Sibun
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Ost Ordura
Location:    Brigand Hall Caverns
Requirement: Complete The Road Patrol

  Follow Ost Ordura into the halls and avoid the traps that are strewn across
your path. Once you cross the first hall, Ost will send you around to open the
gate. Jump down to the east and avoid the traps as you move around to the lever.
With high Detect Hidden you can disarm the traps if you can't dodge them. Move
through the next passageway to spawn some Niskaru. Loot the corpses and check
the [WEAPON RACK], then destroy some crates to find a locked [CHEST].

  Open the door and move east, but beware the bear traps. Search the next camp
for corpses and a [WEAPON RACK] then Ost will stop you. Enter the final camp
and fight the Fahrlangi Cultists and their Archmage. With the summoners down
the Niskaru appear and Ost means an untimely demise. Carry on his task and
loot the [CHEST] in the northern corner. Continue east and when you turn the
corner south start looking out for mine traps.

  Clear out the next camp of the Fahrlangi Swordsman and a Niskaru. Check the
corpses and dispel the three [CHESTS], but again watch out for the mines as
they are craftly placed. Prepare for a challenge in a Niskaru Tyrant, the last
monster of this damned cave. This monster can shoot fireballs and has an array
of attacks. Spells like Storm Bolt that can stun the beast should make it an
easier kill. Loot the [CHEST] to find the [PERFIDIOUS CAP] and loot the Tyrant
for the [PERFIDIOUS GLOVES]. Pick up the [HEART OF SIBUN] and return to
Shieldring Keep then report to Tine Delfric. You receive the [STERN HELM] as
your reward for completing this task and the quest ends.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 Lock and Key
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Tine Delfric
Location:    Shieldring Keep
Requirement: Complete The Heart of Sibun

  To reach Helmgard Keep you need to enter the Plains of Erathel. After the long
trek enter the Keep and speak to Grian Shane. Before setting off on your new
mission take a moment to view the wares of the quartermaster. There are a lot of
+1 and +2 to ability items that can definitely aid you. Head to the southern
junction of Tala-Rane and The Wolds to find the Warsworn Vault. Talk to Gwyn
Anwy then make your way into the Vault.

  The first room is empty but move down the hall to find quite a few Fahrlangi
Mages. Focus on them one at a time then scour the area for quite a few [CHESTS]
On the upper floor you have to unlock a side door to reach the [CHEST], just
beware the Spike Trap. On the opposite side is a Hidden Door with another
[CHEST] behind it. Return to Helmgard Keep and talk with the Castellan. He has
jailed Gwyn so talk to her and get the key, then return to Grian with the
[WARSWORN VAULT KEY].

  Grian wants you to head to the locksmith in Tirin's Rest. It's a long journey
so be prepared before heading off. Enter the Locksmith building and go down into
the lab. Head to the northeast and grab two [CHESTS] then defeat the three
Fahrlangi that strike. Talk to Tefroy Tarion to discover the truth behind the
key then return to Helmgard Keep. Talk to Grian to receive [HAVOC] and start the
next quest.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             The House of No Doors
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Grian Shane
Location:    Helmgard Keep
Requirement: Complete Lock and Key

  Head to the prison cells and speak with Livia Fenan. She confesses everything
and points you towards the Tywili Coast. Inform Grian and leave in search of
Elbin Meroch. Head south of Rathir to find a small camp off the road where you
can find Elbin. Fight him off to gain another clue, then head for Rathir. Enter
the customs house and speak with Oneth at the front desk. Persuade or pay him to
get the password. Head to the Window Grill in the north and use the password,
"Five-and-nine by night." or pass the Persuasion Check to gain access. Likewise,
failing the Persuasion Check throws you into a fight.

  Enter the catacombs and kill the Giant Rats and Fahrlangi that attack. Loot
the [CHEST] and south to find more Fahrlangi, Giant Rats, and a [CHEST]. Watch
out for the Bear Traps and move east to a group of Fahrlangi. Defeat them and
go south to find Mad Harst. A group of Fahrlangi jump out as you realize you've
just been ambushed. All these cultists and swordsman can cast magic so dodge and
block to survive -- using Reckoning is also a fast and efficient closure. Loot
the [CHEST] and go east down the hall to find another. There is a [CHEST] in
the water but it's unmarked, just wade around till you get the option to Dive.

  Resurface and jump off the ledge to enter The Quays. Rendezvous with Gwyn to
complete the quest and receive the [DAUNTLESS CHAUSSES] as well as gold.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              The Isle of Eamonn
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Gwyn Anwy
Location:    Rathir
Requirement: Complete The House of No Doors

  Nearby you can find Captain Fros Gonthorm on the docks. Speak with him and
tell him you're ready to go. Upon arriving you can go left or right, but left is
a dead end and right leads to a Crudok and Venomspitters. Further north are
three Venomspitters and two [CHESTS], one that needs to be dispelled. Along this
circular crossroad are a few more [CHESTS]. Going north spawns Giant Spiders and
Venomspitters but you can find a [SKELETON]. Going east leads to a [CHEST] and
Shrine of Mitharu but coming back you'll encounter two Crudoks.

  To continue, head west and slay the Fahrlangi, starting with the Archmage.
Enter Eammon's Fortress and fight off another group of Fahrlangi. Head up the
steps and fight off two more cultists. There is a Shrine of Mitharu to the south
and more mages to north as you move through the halls. Slay another group of
Fahrlangi Mages and check the Hidden Door to the east where you can discover
three [CHESTS].

  In the southwest corner of this room is a locked [CHEST] that you should loot
before moving west. Kill the mages and loot the [CHEST] to the south. Search the
northern wall for a Hidden Door that leads to a pair of Niskaru Bloodhunters.
Loot the [SKELETONS] in the cages and the [CHEST] along the northern wall.
Backtrack and continue moving west to encounter more mages, led by an Archmage.
Go through the door and into the Chapel where you will encounter wave after
wave of Fahrlangi, swordsman and Archmage alike.

  After the battle loot the [CHEST] in the alcove to find [PEERS OF EAGONN II].
Examine the mural with Gwyn and after some guidance, return to Shieldring Keep.
Confide in Tine to receive a promotion, gold, the [SEEKER'S PLATE], and the
[WARSWORN MONUMENTS KEY] not to mention the fact you just finished the quest.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               The Mystic Hammer
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Tine Delfric
Location:    Shieldring Keep
Requirement: Complete The Isle of Eamonn

  Head into western Alserund to find Eagonn's Tomb. Search the crypt for two
[CHESTS] then approach the tomb to obtain the [MYSTIC HAMMER REMAINS]. With the
item in hand, make the trek east to Ironfast Keep. Head south and find Gwyn who
is eager to forge the hammer. Head to the southwestern corner of Menetyre to
find the Hall of the Firstsworn. Listen to the speech by Gwyn then head east to
find a [CHEST] and a Kobold. Turn the corner and slay a few more Kobold and
snag another [CHEST].

  The next room is large and teeming with Kobold. Go east through the door and
fight off a few more Kobold as you reach a Rock Troll. Go south for now and
slay a few Kobolds then backtrack and go west to find Gwyn's mother. Try to go
through the door, but it is to no avail. After a short speech you can attempt
it once more, this time an animation occurs and you Fateshift the door. Follow
the path to the forge, but first loot the [CHESTS] for the [SKILL BOOK
(BLACKSMITHING)].

  Use the forge and mend the [MYSTIC HAMMER] then talk to Gwyn. The quest ends
as you receive a sum of gold and your final mission.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              The Mountain Prison
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Gwyn Anwy
Location:    Halls of the Firstsworn
Requirement: Complete The Mystic Hammer

  Make the short journey to Cloudcrest in the southeastern Hollowlands. Speak
with Gwyn then enter the passage. Start off heading west and slay the Niskaru
as you approach a group of Fahrlangi and a [CHEST]. Double back and go east to
find more Fahrlangi. As you head south you can enter a small alcove to the north
west with more of the mages and another [CHEST]. Go south and slay a larger
group of mages then proceed west.

  Follow the path north and slay the Niskaru and Fahrlangi combination. You
will encounter the first pillar here and the only way to break it is with the
Mystic Hammer. Progress up to the peak, fell another Niskaru, and break the
second pillar. The next area has the same situation and the third pillar will
fall. Next up are two Niskaru to impede your path to the fourth pillar. The
fifth pillar also has two guardians as does the sixth pillar. Go north and
approach Anru Besin.

|  Anru will have several Fahrlangi along with him but they seem to go down    |
| rather quickly. Once you clear them out a large group of Niskaru will appear |
| but again, they seem to die from only a few attacks. Anru will cast several  |
| unique spells, like an Iceball instead of a fireball and typically keeps his |
| distance. Use a stun to close the distance and pummel through his low armor. |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  After defeating Besin you are given the option of siding with the Warsworn or
with Khamazandu. If you side with the beast and become it's instrument you will
gain the quest [KHAMAZANDU'S GIFT]. If you choose against it then simply loot
the [HELM OF HIDEOUS VISAGE] from Besin and talk to Gwyn. Head for the Hall of
the Firstsworn and approach the group to receive the [TWIST OF FATE - TRUESWORN]
and a bit of gold. It should be noted that this Twist of Fate isn't nearly as
useful as the one you receive for betraying the Warsworn, but at least you are
on good terms with them.
}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               Khamazandu's Gift
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Khamazandu
Location:    Cloudcrest Peak
Requirement: Complete The Mountain Prison
             Become Khamazandu's instrument

  Slay Gwyn Anwy and take the [HELM OF HIDEOUS VISAGE] from Besin's corpse. You
are now tasked with slaying the other Warsworn. Head to the Hall of the
Firstsworn and slay the group. Loot Grian for the [WARSWORN VAULT KEY] then
Fast Travel to the Warsworn Fault. Obtain the [HEART OF SIBUN] to complete the
quest and receive the [TWIST OF FATE - FORSWORN].
}}}

=======================|                                |=======================
                       |     The House of Ballads       |             [09.00.00]
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |________________________________|            
                        ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              Song of Sir Sagrell
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Hallam the White
Location:    House of Ballads

  The first person to slay the Grave Thresh in Gorguath will get a seat in the
House of Ballads, so hop to it. South of the House of Ballads you will find the
entrance to Gorguath. To your immediate right is a [GORGUATH STONE], so read it
and enter the middle section. After the brief scene go south and kill the
Brownies. Continue south to find another [GORGUATH STONE] and a [CHEST] then
backtrack to where you killed the Brownies.

  Go north this time and defeat a larger group of Brownies and take the short
path southeast for a [CHEST]. Stick to the path until you reach the Heartvine
that you need to pull. Go north into a larger with a few Brownies and another
[CHEST]. Continue along the path to the next Heartvine then enter the next area
to the north for a change of pace, Boggarts. There is still a [CHEST] in the
north part of the room but also a Hidden Door that you can see on the minimap
with enough points in Detect Hidden. At the end of the hallway is a third
[GORGUATH STONE].

  Backtrack to the room before this hallway and go northwest to defeat the
Boggarts. Go south to the final Heartvine then clear the remaining Boggarts as
you return to the entrance hall. Go down the center and through the Hidden Door
on the left to reach the bottom layer of all the stuff you just ran around.
Slay the Boggarts and find a few [CHESTS] then return to the center area to face
the Grave Thresh. Fire spells work wonders and the Thresh is rarely stunned, but
the fire can stagger.

  With the creature felled you can loot the [CORPSES] in the corners and a
[CHEST] along the wall. Go north to a [GORGUATH STONE] then loot the corpse in
the middle of the room for the [BALLADS SIGNET RING] and [FAEBLADES OF SONG].
A short scene occurs and a roar of the impending danger should send a warning
sign, another Thresh is coming. Defeat the Thresh in the south and slay the
Boggars to find a [CORPSE]. Clear out the northern area as well then go north
east of the larger room find the last [GORGUATH STONE].

  Loot the [SKELETON] as well then fight your way out of Gorguath. Return to the
House of Ballads and into the Court of Enchantments. Speak with Hallam the White
to conclude this quest.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                            Ballad of Bloody Bones
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Hallam the White
Location:    House of Ballads
Requirement: Complete Song of Sir Sagrell

  You receive a [RESURRECTION POTION] at the start of this quest. Head to the
southern portion of Ettinmere to find the Ballads Oratory. In the center area
you can find King Wencen. Talk to him and check out the [FAE CACHE] before
leaving to Uduath in the northeast corner of Ettinmere. Loot the [CHEST] at the
entrance and go south at the split. Give Sir Farrara a hand with the Sprites
then open the cell. Go west to fight some Brownies, loot a [CHEST], open a cell,
then loot another [CHEST] in the cell area.

  Progress north and kill the Sprites and Brownies then loot the [CHEST] and
open another cell. Continue along the path for more of the same, Brownies, a
[CHEST] and a cell. As you move east watch out for the poison trap. You will
eventually reach the last area with Brownies, a [CHEST], and a cell. Move east
to find Bloody Bones and a [CHEST]. After the conversation kill Bloody Bones and
the Sprites that assist him. Resurrect Farrara then enter the far east room to
find a [FAE CACHE] then leave Uduath and return to the House of Ballads.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                            Two Knights and a Troll
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: King Wencen
Location:    House of Ballads
Requirement: Complete Ballad of Bloody Bones

  You are tasked with a ballad of your own this time. Seek out Tenhwa in the
Ballads Library between Webwood and Haxhi. Tenhwa is in quite a bind but you
can lend her a hand in a bit. Head to the upstairs room and loot the [FAE CACHE]
for the [SKILL BOOK (DISPELLING)]. On the 1st floor you can loot the [TREASURES
OF MEROPIS] off the desk before heading out to Sunder Caverns in north Haxhi.

  Outside of the caverns you can find [TWO KNIGHTS AND A TROLL, PART I] lying
on the ground. Enter Sunder Caverns and talk to Sir Airmer to receive [PART V]
of the series. Go west and north to find two Bears and a [CHEST] then take a
detour west to find three more bears. Continue north and slay the Barghest then
snag [PART III] from the middle of the room. As you move east you can take yet
another detour north and fight off some Barghest before continuing. As you leave
the next room a group of Sprites will surround you, so don't get surprised.

  Follow the path past another group of Sprites and up [PART IV]. Turn the
corner and go a little ways down the corridor to find Nix the Troll. A few
Sprites spawn so put your focus on them while your Fae partners hold off Nix.
Fight Nix like any other Troll and he will soon go down, dropping [PART II] to
complete the Cairns. Loot the two [CHESTS] to the south and make your way back
to the Ballads Library. Use the Echostone in the next room over and play all
the parts of the ballad. Recite the counter-spell and return to the King at the
House of Ballads. The Maid of Windemere has taken over and Hallam has a plan
should you choose to accept it.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               What Lies Beneath
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Hallam the White
Location:    House of Ballads
Requirement: Complete Two Knights and a Troll

  Make the trip to St. Eadric's Mission in The Sidhe and visit Etair. Grave
news when you arrive, Etair is dead. Speak to the monks outside after looting
the [CHEST]. You are guided to the mission well at the north end of the mission.
Descend into the well and search the [CHEST] to the east. Move west and destroy
the Kobolds and loot two more [CHESTS] before heading north. Watch out for the
traps and kill a few Kobolds before progressing past another tripwire trap.

  Defeat the Kobolds in the next area and loot a [CRYSTAL] off the corpses and
check the [CHEST]. Jump off the cliff and slay more Kobolds then wade through
the water to another group of Kobolds. Loot the [CHEST] and the [CRYSTAL] off
the bodies then go north where another [CHEST] is located. Defeat the next group
of Kobolds and loot their bodies for a [CRYSTAL]. There is yet another [CHEST]
in an alcove to the west before you enter more water.

  You can find Brother Wulf on a small island in the water, so hop out and talk
with him. Dispell him to receive the [WHISTLE] then head through the water to
another island. Use the whistle here and loot the last [CRYSTAL] then return to
Hallam the White.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                 The Champions
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Hallam the White
Location:    House of Ballads
Requirement: Complete What Lies Beneath

  You receive a [RESURRECTION POTION] from Hallam and are on your way. To reach
Windemere go to the northeast of Odarath. You will have a short scene with the
Maid of Windemere before you reach Sir Airmer. Choose your opponent but watch
out for the Crudoks that jump into the fray. Loot the unlucky challenger for the
[HOUSE OF BALLADS SET]. Equip the set and move east to fight a Rock Troll that
impedes your path. Climb to the top of the hill to discover you need to find
Sir Elswin's body. Jump down into the water and resurrect Sir Elswin then you
must slay him. Before heading up the ramp again check the water for a [CHEST].

  Cross the gorge and face off with Creth or Airmer and a Thresh. With the foes
downed, enter Summer's End.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Cursed Kingdom
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: The Maid of Windemere
Location:    Summer's End
Requirement: Complete The Champions

  Enter the Chantry after you're done exploring and talk to Sagrell. Step out
and use the whistle to reveal the crystals that must be destroyed. Open the map
and you can see they are in the four corners. They don't stay visible for long
so use the whistle when you are close to reveal the crystal for breaking. When
they are all broken, monsters become hostile again and you need to return to
Sagrell. He will give you the [BELL TOWER KEY] and [HOUSE OF BALLADS SHIELD] and
be on his way.

  Enter the Bell Tower and loot two [CHESTS] then pull the rope and enter Castle
Windemere.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                             The Hero and the Maid
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: The Maid of Windemere
Location:    Castle Windemere
Requirement: Complete Cursed Kingdom

  Check the [WINDEMERE STONE] in front of you and be on your way to savings the
Court of Enchantments. The first member is Sir Farrara who fights with a few
Sprites. Check the southeastern alcove for a [WINDEMERE STONE] before moving on.
Watch out for the venus fly traps as you move into the next room. Fight off the
Boggar Plaguebearers and stay out of the poisonous water while you battle. Go
right and fight off a pair of Leanashe in the library area. Here you can save
Queen Belmaid and Dame Oleyn but the two make a good pairing and two Leanashe
join them. Fire spells will put down the creatures and stuns will keep the
ladies in check.

  Search the southeastern room for a [CHEST] and the north one for the third
[WINDEMERE STONE]. Return to the center room and shoot across, fighting off a
horde of Boggarts. The next room has a [WINDEMERE STONE] visible from the
entrance but everything has poisonous water. You'll likely contract a disease
and you will slowly take damage. The northern room has two [CHESTS] but the
southern one has the King and a [CHEST]. Follow the King back to the main area
and he will unlock the magical barrier.

  You receive the [KING'S TOKEN] and the King leaves. Approach the door and
talk with the Maid of Windemere for the last time.

 ______________________________________________________________________________

|                            The Maid of Windemere                             |

|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|  The Maid will summon a few creatures to aid her but she is pretty powerful  |
| on her own. Her magical attack from her staff can be lethal and the mobs can |
| pile up quickly. Do what damage you can to her and use Reckoning when you    |
| get in trouble to heal quickly and finish her off. The bonus experience from |
| the Reckoning is pretty significant and is definitely the recommended way to |
| end the battle.                                                              |

  Grab the last [WINDEMERE STONE] and leave the castle, returning to the House
of Ballads. Speak with Hallam the White and you receive the [TWIST OF FATE -
ICONOCLAST].

                               The Guided Hands
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Grim Onwig
Location:    Northeast Haxhi

  In northeastern Haxhi you will come across Grim Onwig who will start this
initiation quest. Enter Star Camp and seek out Crilgarin who wants you to pray
at the Hierophant Shrine. Accept the offer and head to Didenhils Three Lamps
Inn. Steal the [GRILRICAS MEDALLION] then head to St. Eadric's Mission. Steal
the [PALL OF ST. EADRIC] from the sarcophagus and make your way down the road
to the Vorm Lodge. Pickpocket [GUNNAR FRODE'S KEY] then go upstairs and unlock
his footlocker to find [GUNNAR FRODE'S MAP].

  Proceed to the northeastern corner of the Sidhe and inspect the pile of rocks
to find [DRAUG'S TOOTHPICKS]. Return to Crilgarin to receive a bunch of handy
tools for a Rogue as well as a chunk of gold.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                The Silent Step
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Hierophant Shrine
Location:    Star Camp
Requirement: Complete The Guided Hands

  Seek out Aergase, Hunting Herald in the Sidhe near Aodh. She informs you that
Ametair is in the Arduath to the north. When you enter you will get a Persuasion
Check from Ametair. Chase after Ametair and attack him; his only attack is to
lunge at you. Continue to run around the area in search of Ametair and each time
he pops out just attack him. If you take damage be sure to heal because you will
incur an endless bleed. Loot [BURU'S BOOTS] from his corpse and search the area
for three [CHESTS].

  Return to Crilgarin to receive some gold and complete the quest.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                   Jailbreak
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Crilgarin
Location:    Star Camp
Requirement: Complete The Silent Step

  Head to Ohn's Stand in southwestern Lorca-Rane. Head west and unlock the gate
to find a [SKELETON]. Turn around and go north this time slaying the enemies
then talking to Grim Onwig. Head to the northeast and open the Hidden Door to
find two [CHESTS]. Take the path southwest to find a Gnomish Sentry in a camp.
Further into the camp you'll battle Sorcerers. You can open the gates and find
[SKELETONS] in them most of the time. When you are done, take the southwest path
that heads southeast to a Centurion Gastet.

  Loot his corpse for the [CENTURION'S KEY] then loot the three [CHESTS] to find
[GRIM'S STEALTH KIT]. Kill the Gnomes ahead then use the [LEVER] to open the
door and return to Grim. You can opt to keep his kit but it's not worth much.
Though Grim is freed, it is worth searching the northern half of the area for
the [CHESTS]. Just beware the Jottun and the Spike Traps along the way. Return
to Crilgarin who is, unfortunately, in no longer need of your services. Head to
Moon Camp as directed for your next task.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              Something Borrowed
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Crilgarin
Location:    Star Camp
Requirement: Complete Jailbreak

  The Moon Camp is just outside of Rathir. Speak to Irion, King of Cups who
seems lost over his love Maire. Pray at the Hierophant Shrine to get the list
of whom you must steal from. Start with the Seafoam Tavern in Rathir where you
can steal the [CHALICE OF FORCED VINTAGE]. The best way to approach this is to
wait at the top of the stairs until Veinrich moves the far bench where you can
sneak up and snag the chalice.

  Stealing the [WYVYRN-GIFRE SIGNET RING] is arguably the easiest one because
you can just stealth behind Ebsol and take the ring. Enter the Temple of Lyria
and speak with Maire, Queen of Cups where you can persuade or purchase the
final piece, the [COWL OF THE MAIDEN]. Return to Irion to receive [IRION'S
WEDDING RING] and complete the quest.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                  Going Rogue
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Irion
Location:    Moon Camp
Requirement: Complete Something Borrowed

  Pray the Hierophant Shrine once again then head to Rithen along the eastern
border of the Tywili Coast. Move through the first room and kill the Freeman
Deserters. Loot the [CHEST] and progress through the hall then open the gate
via the [LEVER]. You get ambushed before you head down the stairs, so be alert.
Approach the gate then use the [LEVER] and continue south. Defeat the Freeman
and loot the three [CHESTS] then stand on the pressure plate in the next room
to gain access to the treasure. Phasmer rushes in and becomes paralyzed!

  Make your way to the entrance, fighting through the Giant Rats, to meet
Grim. He gives you the [TEARS OF MITHARU] that you should use on Phasmer. You
receive the [SKILL BOOK (DETECT HIDDEN)] from Grim Onwig at this time. You also
obtain the [AMULET OF RITHEN] and the quest concludes.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Mirror, Mirror
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Grim Onwig
Location:    Rithen
Requirement: Complete Going Rogue

  Take the alternate exit to find three more [CHESTS]. Kill the Freeman in the
first room and dodge the blades as you ascend the staircase. Use the [LEVER] at
the end to open the Hidden Door and exit. Proceed south along the eastern border
to eventually reach The Blackened Hall. Loot [GRIM'S STASH] and head north to
find a [STONE OF AUTUMN]. Open the door to the east and put on [BURU'S BOOTS].
Run across the spikes and you will be unharmed. Likewise, you can just disarm
the traps and take your time crossing the hall.

  At the far end Buru's Boots wear off. There is another hall with traps but
you can run between them. Fire crashes down towards you so run down the right
side and be fast about it! Use the Erathi Sigil-Stone to difuse the flames then
square off against the Niskaru. Loot the [CHEST] a the southern end for the
[JOURNAL OF SCRIBE PEARSE, VOL. 1]. In the western room you can cross another
trapped floor, but be careful. Sprinting down the row two from the right seems
to get you through unphased, but will require a stutter step right before you
finish crossing.

  Loot the two [CHESTS] and use the far right path going back, applying the same
stutter step to cross unharmed. Enter the eastern hallway and about halfway down
open the Hidden Door to reveal a [CHEST]. As you reach another circular room,
three Niskaru will strike at you from different directions. Head south and slay
another group of Niskaru and loot the [CHEST] at the southern end then progress
north.

  Continue to follow the path as doors open and close around you, limiting your
exploration and choice of direction. At another circular room you will fight
three Niskaru. Follow the path south to another group of Niskaru and a [CHEST].
Turn north past three more Niskaru and west across the hall with another. In
the last room you can find two [CHESTS], one with the [JOURNAL OF SCRIBE PEARSE,
VOL. 3]. Approach The Guardian as it climbs up; it's a Niskaru Tyrant variant.
Defeat this beast and plant the Amulet of Rithen in it then take the [TEAR OF
MITHARU] from it's corpse. Snag the [GLASS AMBIENT] off the altar and make your
way back.

  As you exit you should notice that all the doors are unlocked now. Just before
reaching the second circular room turn south to find a [CHEST] with [THE JOURNAL
OF SCRIBE PEARSE, VOL.2] inside. From the second circular room head north to
find a [CHEST]. Return to the entrance and speak with Grim for your reward.
}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                Outside the Box
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Grim Onwig
Location:    The Blackened Halls
Requirement: Complete Mirror, Mirror

  Make the incredibly long trip to Sun Camp on the eastern border of Apotyre.
Speak with Argine, Queen of Staves and tell her you're looking for work. Pray
at the Hierophant Shrine then head to Adessa. Make your way to the Laboratories
and steal the [NOTICE OF SEIZURE] and [CRIET'S BURSARY KEY] from Eloren Criet
who is usually on the upper floors waltzing around. Leave the labs and enter the
Armory.

  Inside you can pickpocket the [ARMORY MASTER KEY] from the Praetorian. You
need to sneak around and there are plenty of things to loot from and easy
opportunities to move down the main hall. At the end of the hall is the [CHEST]
you care about though, for it holds the [ORNATE BOX]. Return to Argine who is
quite upset about this box. Head out north to the Motus Mining Headquarters.
Talk to Guian who humbly refuses then search the northern cobwebbed room for a
[CHEST] containing the [KEY TO MAYOR'S VILLA].

  Go down the steps and break into the lab. Follow the path to a chamber filled
with Faer Gorta. In the southwest corner is a [CHEST] as well as the northeast.
Exit southeast to a room with spike traps, a [CHEST], and the Arrivus Engine.
Return to Argine with the [MASTER'S KEY] to complete the quest and receive a
bunch of gold.
}}}

                             Classic Misdirection
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Argine
Location:    Sun Camp
Requirement: Complete Outside the Box

  Pray at the Hierophant Shrine to receive your orders then leave the Sun Camp
and head north into Convict's Cavern. Watch out for the traps as you reach
Cointaker. Tell him your purpose to receive [MAUN'S KEY] and the location of his
treasures. Go west to Snaketail Grotto, likely guarded by Kobolds and Darkvari.
Check the corpses and the [CHEST] then go west to find Zungar and Darkvari
dueling. Slay the foes and search the [LOOT PILE] to the north. At the southern
end is another Darkvari and a [LOOT PILE] in the corner, opposite this is an
unmarked [SKELETON].

  Cross all the way over to the east side and open a door to find a [LOOT PILE]
behind some crates. Come back to the center and proceed south. At the split go
east to find a [LOOT PILE] in the corner behind a door. Go south from here and
kill the Zungar, loot the [CHEST] for the [ZUNGAR KEY], and search the [MINING
CART]. Return to the split and go west this time, defeating the Zungar and the
Darkvari as they fight.

  At the southern end you can find two [CHESTS], one with the [DARKVARI KEY]
inside. Go to the end of the eastern path to find the another [CHEST] and a
[SKELETON]. Head back north a ways and turn west towards a gate that you can
now unlock. Loot the final [CHEST] and take [MAUN'S NOTE]. On your way out you
should encounter Grim Onwig who gives you 10 [GRIM'S SPECIAL] and concludes the
quest.

}}}

                             The Purloined Letters
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Grim Onwig
Location:    Snaketail Grotto
Requirement: Complete Classic Misdirection

  Head to Adessa and rendezvous with Phasmer in the Livrarium. After the brief
you receive the [SHROUD OF OMISSION]; head into the Livrarium Vaults. Down the
hall you'll encounter a Sentry, loot the corpse for a [REMIND FOR INITIATES].
Take the southwest path to find the Keymaster - kindly remove the [VAULT KEY]
from his corpse. Check the [CHEST] at the end of this room and return to the
initial one.

  Head straight across and unlock the door with the key. Deal with the Sentries
then pull the [LEVER] to reveal a way out into the Forum. Ignore it for now
and continue southeast through the door. Kill the Sentry and move into the next
room. Open the gate to the northeast to find some [CHESTS] and a lot of crates.
Continue the path deeper into the vaults to find Giants Rats and a [CHEST]
behind all the crates. Continue around until you reach the sleeping quarters
where two Keymasters are resting. Slay them and use the [LEVER] to return to the
center room.

  Unlock the southeastern door and move down the hall. Enter the northeastern
room to find a Sentry and a [CHEST]. Return to the main hall, go southeast and
kill two Sentries. There is a [CHEST] along the walls and a southwestern exit.
Paths converge on the next room where a [CHEST] that requires some work to
unlock. Use the braziers in the order below.

                           [1]   [2]         1. Activate 1, then 2.
                                             2. Activate 4, then 5.
                       [8]           [3]     3. Activate 7, then 8.
                                             4. Activate 3, then 6.
                       [7]           [4]

                           [6]   [5]

  Loot the [CHEST] to get a [VAULT KEY] then continue southwest. Slay the two
Sentries and grab four [CHESTS], one in each corner of the room. Inspect the
[MISSIVES OF SABLE] and wrap it, then fight your way back to the ladder leading
to the forum. Head to the Hospitalis Quarters where Grim Onwig awaits you. Your
reward is the [SKILL BOOK (STEALTH)] and a hefty sum of gold.

}}}

                               Thick as Thieves
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Grim Onwig
Location:    Adessa - Hospitalis Quarters
Requirement: Complete The Purloined Letters

  Enter the Sun Camp and use the secret entrance to the Hierophant's Den. Argine
will approach you and give the [SANCTUM KEY]. You have the option of framing
Grim or Argine. For now go south and loot the [PILE] and meet up with Crilgarin.
Fight through Argine's Guards in the next room and loot a [CHEST] and [WEAPON
RACK] before going south. Defeat another group of guards and loot two more
[CHESTS] before ascending the ramp.

  Sneak up on this last guard and steal the [BAG OF WINDS] then loot the area.
Head back to the north and when you reach the room with the giant statue, use
the Bag of Winds and simply cross over into the Sanctum. Loot the [CHEST] and
choose a wing.

Eastern Wing (Frame Grim Onwig)
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Slay Argine's Guards then sneak up on Grim Onwig and frame him. Break the pots
and jump down, heading north past some of Sentries. Drop down into the next area
where Guards and Sentries are fighting. Kill them and loot Crilgarin then search
the two side rooms for [CHESTS] and [PILES], just beware the pressure plates
that release spinning blades. Meet with Argine and kill the Sentries in the next
room. Loot the [CHEST] in the back then head up the stairs. You receive the
[TWIST OF FATE - TEMPERANCE] and the entire [SHADOWSKIN SET]. The Twist of Fate
gives you +1 to Finesse and +6% Evade Chance.

Western Wing (Frame the Hierophant)
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Kill Argine's Guard and proceed to Argine. Sneak up and plant the Missives
then break the nearby pots and jump down. Head north and fend off the Sentries
as you meet up with Phasmer. Further along you can help Crilgarin kill the rest
of the guards. Join up with Grim a little further then clear the final room.
Loot the [CHEST] and head up the steps to receive [TWIST OF FATE - THE CHARIOT]
which grants +1 to Finesse and +6% Piercing Damage. You also receive the entire
[SHADOWSKIN SET].
