                                 Trial by Fire
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Docent Augra Tenet
Location:    Scholia Arcana

  Speak with the Docent and ask to join the Scholia Arcana. You receive [AN
ORNATE KEY] and the book [THE SCHOLIA ARCANA] and can now undergo the Trial of
Initiation. Enter the Delving Hall and dispel the two [CHESTS] in large room.
Proceed north through the doorway and talk to Aethan Engar. Step into the
circle when you are ready to be taken to your trial.

  Slay the Faer Gorta and head south up the steps to find another group. Go
through the doors and fight off more Faer Gorta -- don't bypass the [CHEST]
before you complete the first phase. Loot the [OVERTURNED CART] then head
through the waterfall and slay the Tuatha. Cross the bridge to find two more
soldier and as you move towards a town Engar begins to lose touch with you.
Clear out the Tuatha and speak with the Sorceress to return from the Trial.
Speak with Aethen Engar to get some understanding and receive [THE KEY TO AODH]
and the [NEOPHYTE'S RING].

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               The Ruin of Aodh
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Aethan Engar
Location:    Delving Hall
Requirement: Complete Trial by Fire

  Snag the [CHEST] at the northern end before heading down the hallway. There
are two [CHESTS] in the main room and the book [AODH] is now lootable. Head to
Aodh in the center of the Sidhe and proceed along the path until you encounter
some Sprites. Keep in mind that most enemies in this area are fire resistant,
like the Flame Champion Sprite. Loot the [SKELETON] and continue, watching out
for the Fire Mines. On the next platform are four Fire Mines and a [CHEST].

  Finish crossing the platform and slay two Sprites as you enter the halls
with Arcane Barghest and Priests of Vraekor. Check the eastern and northern
rooms then continue south past a Fire Mine. Slay a group of Sprites and enter a
room filled with mines. Stealth through them or just pick them up (if you have
that skill) and loot the [SKELETON] at the far end before opening the door.

  There is a mine in the middle of this floor and two side rooms with [CHESTS]
guarded by tons of mines. At the crossroads go east into a room with a [CHEST].
Sprites appear as you loot it so kill them and check the [SKELETON] along the
wall guarded by Fire Mines. The southern room has a High Priest and two normal
Priests of Vraekor, the former holds [THE PRIMER OF FIRE]. Loot the [CHEST] and
move west to another group of Sprites.

  Slay the flying beasts and move past a single mine as you move to a narrower
hallway filled with them. Loot the [CHEST] in the corner and go north to find
two Shrines and Nuala Ignas. The witch is fire resistant and summons Sprites
to her dirty work. Dodge the few spells she throws at you and loot the two
[CHESTS] for the [BOOTS OF THE DARK EMPYREAN] and her corpse for the [SUN
STONE]. Follow the path out and don't pass the two [CHESTS] before returning to
Engar.
}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               The Unquiet Bride
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Aethan Engar
Location:    Ysa
Requirement: Complete The Ruin of Aodh

  Head to the Plains of Erathell, particularly Tala-Rane. On the eastern border
you can find Jubal Caledus at the scene of a massacre. Aid Jubal in defeating
the Assassins to receive the [LETTER FROM LERKARA]. Continue to Mel Aglir in
Kandrian and enter The Raven. Speak with Patrick Morkan then head up the steps
and loot the [FOOTLOCKER] for [LERKARA's JOURNAL]. Read the journal to update
the quest then head to the northwest corner of eastern Kandrian.

  Slay the Kobolds along the trip and enter Tulan. Beware the Bear Traps as you
progress towards three Kobolds. North through the hall are more traps and a few
Kobolds enter the fray. Further along are more Kobolds and a split path. Go east
first to find a [CHEST] and a group of Kobold. Pass the Poison Mines and jump
down to fight some Faer Gorta. Around the corner you can find Lerkara Fel and
a [CHEST].

  After the information has been acquired head to the next room to find Patrick
Morkan. Slay the couple and loot the corpses for [PATRICK MORKAN'S KEY] then
take the quick exit out to Patrick's house. Raid the [CHEST] on the top floor
for gems and unlock the desk to acquire a book. Return to the Raven and speak
with Lerkara then go to Rathir to find Aethan Engar in the main hall at the
Scholia Arcana. You receive the [DOCENT'S RING] and the quest ends.
}}}

                                   Shardfall
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Aethan Engar
Location:    Rathir - Scholia Arcana
Requirement: Complete The Unquiet Bride

  Head north to Emaire and enter the Edmure home. Speak with Anker to learn
about Shardfall. Go north and slay a Paragon Barghest and loot it for [A
BARGHEST'S BEATING HEART] then return to Anker to get the [PENDANT OF WARMTH].
Enter Shardfall at the northwest of the Cradle of Summer. Go south and kill the
Sprites and check the [LOOT PILE] before turning west. Watch out for the Ice
Mines as you kill the Bear and Wolf that charge down the hall.

  Kill a few more Wolves and check the next [LOOT PILE] as you continue west.
Be mindful of the Ice Mines and follow the path until you can turn north to
find a [LOOT PILE]. Further ahead you will find a group of Sprites and a [LOOT
PILE] surrounded by Ice Mines. Ahead is a Mountain Troll with four Ice Mines
grouped in the center of the room. You can tag the Troll and run around the
circle to pull it through the mines to take significant damage.

  Proceed north to a group of Wolves and a Bear. There is a Hidden Door to the
west which leads to a [SKELETON] and a few [DIVE POINTS]. Backtrack and head
east to find Donnel Cutty; approaching the corpse spawns Sprites. Loot Donnel
for [DONNEL CUTTY'S RING]. Follow the path until you can jump down and find
Cadoc Reen. Slay the possessed and loot the corpse for the [GRASP OF THE DARK
EMPYREAN] and the [FROST STONE]. Search the [LOOT PILE] to the north and leave
the cave.

  Talk to Anker Edmure and choose the dialogue option for Donnel Cutty. You'll
give up the ring in exchange for some [GEM CUTTING HANDWRAPS]. Return to the
Scholia Arcana in Rathir and speak with Eran Methneen. You will receive the
[ADEPT'S RING] and [AETHAN ENGAR'S LETTER] as the quest concludes.

}}}

                             Lightning in a Bottle
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Eran Methneen
Location:    Rathir - Scholia Arcana
Requirement: Complete Shardfall

  Make your way to Skycrown and slay the Ettin Warpriest and Shaman outside the
entrance. Much like the other ruins, this one is attuned to an element - that
being Lightning. Defeat the enemies in this room and search the western wall
for a [CHEST]. Watch out for the Lightning Mines as you head northwest up the
stairs. Defeat the Ettin and follow the path past a few piles of Mines. Kill
the Sprites before going through the door and fighting more.

  Loot the [CHEST] before going up the steps and opening another [CHEST] that
holds the [ROBES OF THE DARK EMPYREAN]. Go to the Skycrown Peak and fight
through the Ettin and Wolves. Loot the [CHEST] to the north and continue going
east. Slay a few more Ettins and Wolves and check the [CHEST] in the corner. As
the path turns south you'll encounter more enemies and another [CHEST] along
the eastern boundary.

  Pummel the Ettin in the camp and loot the [CHEST] then proceed south. Snag a
[CHEST] before going up the stairs to meet Engar. After the scene turn north
and jump down a level. Loot the [SKELETON] and the [CHEST] then backtrack out
of the cavern. Go in search of Engar's body but when you get to where it should
have landed it is missing. Head to the southern portion of west Kandrian to
find Aethan Engar. Slay him and the Sprites that are summoned then loot the
[SUN STONE] and the [STORM STONE]. Return to Eran Methneen to conclude the
quest.

}}}

                                A Crowded Mind
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Eran Methneen
Location:    Rathir - Scholia Arcana
Requirement: Complete Lightning in a Bottle

  Head east into the Archmage Quarters and place your hand on the corpse to be
taken to another dream-like world. Speak with Jubal Caledus to gain some insight
and [THE DARK EMPYREAN] book. Head east and dispel [THE POSSESSION BEGINS] box
to gain the [MANTLE KEY] and [THE POSSESSION BEGINS] document. At the fork you
will engage two Ancient Leanashe and can locate [THE MANTLE PASSES] chest to
obtain the [PATRONAGE KEY] and [THE MANTLE PASSES] document.

  Turn north and slay a pair of Ettin then open [AN ODD PATRONAGE] chest and
take the [LEFT KEY] and [AN ODD PATRONAGE]. At the end of this path you will
meet with Caledus' Indifference. Three Niskaru spawn and must be defeated, then
Indifference will strike but is easily felled. Unlock [THE WORLD I LEFT] to get
the [TALENT KEY] and [THE WORLD I LEFT]. Go south and kill the Faer Gorta and
loot the [SKELETONS] then unlock [THE HUMAN'S TALENT] to receive the [FLAME KEY]
and [THE HUMAN'S TALENT].

  Cross the mystical bridge to the east to find Caledus' Ambition. Defeat the
Sacrifices first then loot [THE WILD FLAME]. Return to the Archsage and choose
your path, [TWIST OF FATE - FEARLESS] or [TWIST OF FATE - DISCIPLINED]. Fearless
grants a damage bonus while disciplined grants a resistance bonus, they both
grant +1 to Sorcery. Tell the Archsage you are ready to return and head north
into the Main Hall. Talk to Jubal to receive the [SAVANT'S RING] and start the
final quest for this faction.

                                  Revelation
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Jubal Caledus
Location:    Rathir - Scholia Arcana
Requirement: Complete A Crowded Mind

  Place the Storm Stone on the western statue, the Frost Stone in the eastern
statue, and the Sun Stone in the southern statue. This will summon Ciara and
she won't back down.

 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                                Ciara Sydanus                                 |
|                                                                              |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
|  Ciara will use a spell off the start that places large red circles on the   |
| ground. Touching one will cause it to explode and severely damage you. As    |
| you whittle Ciara's life past 75% she will summon Possessed Students that    |
| cast spells. During this time Ciara won't attack much so clear out the       |
| students and then resume attacking Ciara. As her health cross 50%, Ciara     |
| summons Faer Gorta to aid her and will continue to do so until she reaches   |
| 25% health. Ciara now will cast fireballs and waves of fire while floating   |
| high in the air, she also summons two more Possessed Students that should be |
| immediately slain. Focus on using Lightning-based attacks and take her down  |
| for good this time.                                                          |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
  Loot Ciara for the [COWL OF THE DARK EMPYREAN]. Speak with Eran Methneen and
you become the Archsage, thus acquiring the [ARCHSAGE'S RING] and [A LETTER FROM
ARCHSAGE CALEDUS].
}}}

                       |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |     The House of Sorrows       |             [12.00.00]
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |________________________________|            
                        ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               The Sorrows Call
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Bisarane
Location:    Junction of Cursewood and the Midden

  Accept the quest for the House of Sorrows and head to the Proving Halls in
the Midden. Kill the Boggarts and the Leanashe that attack you in the first
room and loot the [CHEST] before moving east. Speak with Taibreah in the next
room and kill the Warpriest and Boggarts the attack. Loot the [CHEST] and keep
moving.

  Speak with Bisarane in the next room and choose an answer that befits you.
Kill the Bog Thresh and Boggarts, loot the [PILE], and continue north. Loot the
[CHEST] in the alcove and open the door. Talk with Cadoroc and set him free then
move west after looting the [CHEST]. Kill the Bog Thresh and move to the next
room where you meet Bisarane in person. Loot the [CHEST] after the conversation
as the quest ends.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                              Voices of the Dead
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Bisarane
Location:    Proving Halls
Requirement: Complete The Sorrows Calls

  Enter the House of Sorrows and speak with Bisarane. Escort Taibreah through
the Midden past the Leanashe, Boggarts, and Barghest. Protect her while she
performs the ritual then go south into the Drowned Forest to reach the Sioran
Crypt. Slay the Sprites in the first room and go through the Hidden Door. Kill
the Spiders at the bottom of the stairs and loot the [CHEST]. This route ends
up being a shortcut to Cadoroc. Slay the Fae and unlock the [CHEST] before
moving east.

  Slay the Giant Spiders that ambush you then loot the [CHEST] in the corner.
Go up the stairs to find two more [CHESTS] and three Sprites that try to stop
you from looting them. Follow the path to a Bog Thresh and bunch of Boggarts.
Kill them then search the [CHEST] before turning the corner. Take out a few more
Boggarts as you loot another [CHEST] and exit the crypt. Return to Taibreah to
receive the full [HOUSE OF SORROWS SET] and the bad news that comes with it.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                A House Divided
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Taibreah
Location:    Outside the House of Sorrows
Requirement: Complete Voices of the Dead

  Make your way to the Proving Halls and fight through it as Bolgan now inhabit
these halls. Once you make it back to the House of Sorrows seek out Bisarane.
Make your way to the Fallen Hall in the southeastern corner of the Keening. Go
through the door and fight off the Tuatha. Move south and slay more Tuatha as
you enter a short scene. Use the Erathi Sigil-Stone then move southeast to fight
a Troll. Finish the Tuatha inside the room and dispel the [CHEST] then use the
second Erathi Sigil-Stone.

  Return to the center path and move west as you slay the Tuatha in your way.
Enter the room at the end of the hallway and kill the Tuatha. Loot the [CHEST]
and use the final Erathi Sigil-Stone then return to the central path. Move south
into the previously inaccessible area and defeat the Tuatha that lurk. Dispel
the [CHEST] and go through the hallway where you get ambushed. At the end of the
hallway you will confront Myrcyr. Tuatha will pour into this room so defeat
Myrcyr as swiftly as possible. Loot the two [CHESTS] and use the Hidden Door to
find a tree and two [SKELETONS] lying on the floor.

  Leave the Fallen Hall and return to Bisarane at the House of Sorrows. You will
receive the [ROBES OF SORROW] as a reward.
}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                  The Eldest
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Bisarane
Location:    House of Sorrows
Requirement: Complete A House Divided

  You receive the [DAMALROC SCALES KEY] and are on your way south to Damalroc
in the Caeled Coast. Check the southern portion of the entrance room and empty
the [CHEST]. Go east and square off against some Sprites then turn right at the
crossroads. Clear out the Sprites in the circular room and exit to the northwest
to find a [CHEST] in the room. Return to the crossroads, taking the opposite
path this time.

  Rid the room of Sprites and dispel the [CHEST] in the other room. Move into
the central room and slay the Banshaen and Murghan. Check the [STONE OF AUTUMN]
underneath the steps then proceed up the stairs and use the Damalroc Scales Key
to unlock the door. Slay the Murghan in the hall and proceed into the next room
where you can find a [CHEST} and an Erathi Sigil-Stone. Use it twice and slay
the Murghan both times to release the doors.

  Follow the path to Alarane and listen to her words. Agree to find her second
half then empty the [CHEST] and move into the next room to find another [CHEST]
in the corner. Return to the Erathi Sigil-Stone and bypass the scale once more.
Move through the halls and loot the [CHEST] before speaking with Caelrod. Move
to the center to receive the [SORROWS TALISMAN] then choose either Caelrod or
Alarane to join you on the journey.

}}}
 _____________________________________________________________________________
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               The Weeping King
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Caelrod
Location:    Damalroc
Requirement: Complete The Eldest

  In the southern corner of the Caeled Coast you can find Sinsear. Meet with
your companion to receive the [VOTIVE OF STONE] then move north. Kill the
Boggarts and dispel the [CHEST] then exit via the eastern path. In the next room
you will encounter a Bog Thresh that holds the [VOTICE OF LEAF]. Again, go east
and defeat a Sprite Flame Champion and it's companions for the [VOTIVE OF FLAME]
then move through the watery path.

  Defeat the Banshaen in the next room for the [VOTIVE OF WATER]. Empty the
nearby [CHEST] then move west into the next room where Sprites ambush you. Loot
the [CHEST] to the south then go north and use the levers in the order; Left,
Right, Center. Check the [CHEST] underneath this area and move north to another
[CHEST] and [A WITHERED BRANCH]. Return to Bisarane in the House of Sorrows then
fight off the Tuatha and Myrcyr to receive the [CROWN OF THE WEEPING KING].

}}}

¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                               Such Sweet Sorrow
_______________________________________________________________________________
 ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Quest Giver: Bisarane
Location:    House of Sorrows
Requirement: Complete The Weeping King

  Speak with Taibreah and go to Esharra. Move west to face Caelrod and a
Leanashe then dispel the first nexus. Go north to find Alarane, kill her then
dispel the second nexus. Follow the path east to fight Myrcyr and dispel the
third nexus. The final nexus is guarded by Cadoroc and a few spiders. Confront
Bisarane for the final showdown.

}}}

Quest Giver: Jakin Madsen
Location:    House of Valor

  Speak with Tyr Magnus and check the Hidden Fireplace to reveal [CHESTS] with

===============================================================================
                                Alabastra Stone
===============================================================================

- West of Camp Moondown in an alcove.
- Along the southern road of Shadow Pass.
- Along road in southern Shadow Pass between the entrances of Mordus-Torr.
- At the entrance of Twilight Pass.
- On the other side of the large fence as you approach the Eventide in Twilight
  Pass.

===============================================================================
                                Alserund Stone
===============================================================================

- Far east near a Shrine of Thyrdon under a rocky platform before the House of
  Valor.
- East of Fellfire Pit
- Western side of Alserund, south of the Caverns of Ingress and east of Pura.
- Along the eastern border just off the road to Menetyre.
- West of the Fellfire Pit in the southwestern corner on a cliff.

===============================================================================
                                 Amaura Stone
===============================================================================

- Outside the southern Cann-Rane entrance.
- Camp north of the southern Cann-Rane entrance.
- West of the rendezvous point, south of the Prismere Basin.
- Outside of the Prismere Basin.
- Ouside of the northern Cann-Rane entrance.

===============================================================================
                                 Apotyre Stone
===============================================================================

- On the bottom level next to the Cynric Quarry.
- East of Skoria Mine along the river.
- Junction of Menetyre and Apotyre.
- Outside the Zungar Mine
- North of Whitestone in a narrow alcove.

===============================================================================
                                 Bhaile Stone
===============================================================================

- Just past the circle where you meet up with Alyn Shir.
- After the first camp along the path.
- Island after the first bridge.
- South of where you fight the Prismere Troll in the northern half of Bhaile.
- In the northwest corner just off the road before entering the Court of Winter.

===============================================================================
                              Caeled Coast Stone
===============================================================================

- Southwest corner of northern Caeled Coast.
- West of Odi's Camp along the northern border.
- In the junction of north and south Caeled Coast.
- North of Castle Ansilla along the road.
- North of Sinsear

===============================================================================
                            Cradle of Summer Stone
===============================================================================

- Off the side of the road at the juncture with the Forsaken Plain.
- On the juncture with the Forsaken Plain.
- As you enter the Cradle of Summer head due west to the southern of the two
  jump points.
- In the southeastern corner just north of Syl.
- East of Urul-Tusk in-between the two rivers at the top of the waterfall.

===============================================================================
                               Dalentarth Stone
===============================================================================

- In Odarath after speaking with Agarth and choosing your fate.
- Second Red Legion Camp in northern Odarath
- Inside the Caer Nyralim along the road.
- Inside The Gardens of Ysa, to the north along the entrance road.
- South of Brunuath in Lorca-Rane, along the river.

===============================================================================
                                Ettinmere Stone
===============================================================================

- Just off the road as you enter Ettinmere.
- South of Holnstead on a cliff guarded by Barghest.
- On a small island in the southeast, just north of the southern road.
- Island in the northwest guarded by Boggarts and a Thresh.
- Outside Dellach during the Main Quest Into the Light.

===============================================================================
                                 Galafor Stone
===============================================================================

- East of Skycrown and west of Gloamthicket on a cliff.
- Along the northern junction to the Tywili Coast.
- At the north section of the Tywili Coast before entering Galafor.
- On a cliff to the west of Tirin's Rest near a burned down home.
- East of the farm in the northern section of Galafor.

===============================================================================
                                Glendara Stone
===============================================================================

- In Glendara, southwest of the Shrine of Ynadon just off the road.
- By the west bridge of Didenhil near a jump point and a waterfall.
- East of Didenhil along the river. Guarded by a Bear.
- North of Coilsbain Caverns and south of Hunter's Pit - East.
- East of Ironhold Passage in southern Glendara.

===============================================================================
                                Gorguath Stone
===============================================================================

- Inside Gorguath at the first alcove on the right.
- Southeast corner of Gorguath near a chest
- Follow the path through the Hidden Door in the northwest room.
- North of the Grave Thresh.
- Northern most room in an eastern alcove.

===============================================================================
                                  Haxhi Stone
===============================================================================

- South of Haxhi Dam just off the road.
- Southern-most part of Haxhi near a group of Murghan.
- In the southeast just outside of Splitrock Depths.
- Centrally located, just west of the Shrine of Ethene.
- Northwest of the previous Stone and guarded by Sprites.

===============================================================================
                                Kandrian Stone
===============================================================================

- South of Caer Tosai on the cliff.
- East of Derfel's House and Tam's Wagon on the cliff.
- In the middle of Mel Aglir
- Junction between east and west Kandrian.
- East of Mel Aglir along the river.

===============================================================================
                                Menetyre Stone
===============================================================================

- West of Ironfast Keep in the river.
- North of the Hermit Smith in central Menetyre
- On the cliff in the south where the Hermit Smith is located.
- Along the eastern border just north of the junction to Apotyre.
- Upper level of the zone near a Shrine of Mitharu.

===============================================================================
                                Odarath Stone
===============================================================================

- Outside of Agnur Farhal.
- On a small island in the northwest of Odarath
- North of Gorhart in the south western section near Aery.
- East half of Odarath, north of Gorguath.
- North of Gorguath and east of the Shrine of Lyria near a massive tree.

===============================================================================
                                Stone of Autumn
===============================================================================

- Inside Agnur Farhal. North at the four-way crossing with 4 Brownies.
- Inside Agnur Farhal. In the last room between two crates.
- Inside the Blackened Hall. In the first hall at the northern end.
- Inside Mull-Rane, southeast room.
- Inside Mull-Range, northwest room.
- In the depths of Foes' Hearth.
- Inside Damalroc under the steps in the room with Banshaen.
- Inside Mordus-Torr, central area.
- Inside Weconai, along the path going west
- Inside Weconai, in a room to the south.

===============================================================================
                               Stone of Klurikon
===============================================================================

- Along the northern road near the junction to the Midden.
- South from the previous Lorestone along the eastern border of Cursewood.
- Outside of Ghennig in the Keening.
- Outside of Bonnlach in the west half of the Drowned Forest.
- South of Odi's Camp in the Caeled Coast.

===============================================================================
                                Stone of Spring
===============================================================================

- In the east half of Odarath along the river, south of Gorguath.
- Along the path from Webwood to Ettinmere
- Northwest corner of Lorca-Rane, south of Brigand Hall Caverns
- Along the path from The Hollowlands to Menetyre.
- In the west half of the Forsaken Plain, south of the Windstone in the north
  eastern corner.
- Northeast corner west east Kandrian.
- South of Virki in the Tywili Coast.
- In a Freeman Camp on the eastern border of eastern Forsaken Plains.
- East of Culn in the Tywili Coast along the border.
- In southern Alserund, north of Caer Elatha.

===============================================================================
                                Stone of Summer
===============================================================================

- On the road between east and west Odarath.
- Northern tip of Webwood just east of the path joining to Yolvan.
- At the entrance to Adessa
- East of Warden's Bridge in Lorca-Rane
- In the northeast of east Kandrian along the border.
- East of Emaire near the junction of east and west Forsaken Plains.
- North of the Bitter Cove in eastern Forsaken Plain.
- East of Deep Slumber along the river.
- Southwestern part of Acatha, just east of Skycrown.
- Along the upper level of Menetyre to the far east.

===============================================================================
                                Stone of Winter
===============================================================================

- Southeast of Mel Senshir just off the road.
- Southwest corner of the Keening, outside of Rahnil.
- Northern tip of the Drowned Forest, west of Sioran Crypt.
- In southern Caeled Coast outside the House of Pride.
- Along the road from High Fulgen into Shadow Pass.
- In Shadow Pass, to the east of the last camp in front of a Hidden Door.
- Just east of Ashmoor in the Twilight Pass, guarded by Sprites.
- Outside the House of Vengeance in Amaura.
- North of where you fight the Prismere Troll in Bhaile.
- Northwest of Tinehil in the Midden.

===============================================================================
                           Stone of the Hollowlands
===============================================================================

- North east of the Saltwell Caverns (On the "W" in the Map)
- South eastern corner on the way to Menetyre.
- Just around the corner to the north from the previous Stone.
- To the west of the Motus Mining Outpost near Calovar.
- Alcove southeast of Shadowthorn where you slay Bloodbane.

===============================================================================
                              Stone of the Midden
===============================================================================

- South the Proving Halls.
- Northern section of the Midden above the waterfall where Taibreah performs
  a ritual.
- East of the Proving Halls along the water.
- North of Meathgra's Den on a cliff.
- East of Meathgra's Den and north of a Hidden Door along the river.

===============================================================================
                           Stone of the Red Marches
===============================================================================

- Southwest of Galette on a ridge.
- Outside the Galette Tunnels.
- Northeast corner on the highest level.
- Eastern side of the Red Marches, accessed via the Tomb of Fyragnos.
- Southern part of the Red Marches, accessed by the southern exit of the Tomb.

===============================================================================
                              Stone of the Sidhe
===============================================================================

- South of the Vorm Inn along the river and next to a jump point.
- South of Aodh and north of Rundamir near two jump points.
- East of Aodh
- In the east part of the Sidhe in the water before Ysa.
- To the south, east of Rundamir, past a pack of Brownies in a watery alcove.

===============================================================================
                              Stone of the Wolds
===============================================================================

- In the graveyard as you enter the Wolds.
- Along the road just before the juncture into the Forsaken Plain
- At the northern junction of the Wolds and Tala-Rane
- East of Cranalt along the river.
- Near a Freeman camp at the southern juncture of Tala-Rane.

===============================================================================
                              Summer's End Stone
===============================================================================

- North of east Odarath just before Windemere.
- Southern part of Windemere across the river before the Bridge.
- Northwest of the town in Summer's End.
- Eastern corner of Summer's End.
- South of Summer's End near the river.

===============================================================================
                                Tala-Rane Stone
===============================================================================

- East of Corgan Hold on a cliff.
- Cave in the southwest were you find Rotclaw.
- East of Dolve Wayle
- South the giant Windstone, right along the road to Kandrian.
- South of Dolve Wayle, high on a cliff.

===============================================================================
                                 Webwood Stone
===============================================================================

- Southeastern tip of Webwood that connects to Haxhi.
- South-central tip of Webwood past a small camp.
- Southwestern corner of Webwood just north of Shade River Caves.
- West of Canneroc along the river, just off the main road.
- Southern corner of Haxhi/Webwood near the Togh Farm.

===============================================================================
                                Windemere Stone
===============================================================================

- First room of Castle Windemere.
- Second room of Castle Windemere in the southeastern alcove.
- Southeastern room with Queen Belmaid.
- Northwestern room filled with poison.
- Final room after defeating the Maid.

===============================================================================
                                 Yolvan Stone
===============================================================================

- Initial room in Castle Yolvan
- Up the ramp from the initial room.
- Northeast corner of Castle Yolvan.
- Northwest corner of Castle Yolvan.
- Southwest corner of Castle Yolvan.

}}}

=======================|                                |=======================
                       |          Skill Books           |             [15.00.00]
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |________________________________|            
                        ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
Alchemy       - Behind the Hidden Door in the Cradle of Summer in a Pile of
                Rocks.
Blacksmithing - In the Halls of the Firstsworn in the forge room. You must be on
                the quest The Mystic Hammer to enter this area.
Detect Hidden - Receive from Grim Onwig after completing Going Rogue.
Dispelling    - Inside the Fae Cache on the second floor of the Ballads Library.
                This cannot be accessed until you have obtained the Ballads
                Signet Ring from the quest Song of Sir Sagrell.
Lockpicking   - First chest on the left as you enter Orieator's Tomb in the
                Forsaken Plains.
Mercantile    - On a Bookshelf in Aron's Mining Shack.
Persuasion    - Complete the quest Paper Trail to receive this as your reward.
Sagecraft     - Inside a Hidden Well in the northern part of Glendara to the
                east of St. Hadwyn's Mission.
Stealth       - Receive from Grim Onwig after completing The Purloined Letter.

}}}

                       |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |           Trainers             |             [16.00.00]
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |________________________________|            
                        ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
{{{
  There are four trainers for each skill which translates into a four additional
points that you don't have to spend. If you happen to exceed the requirements
you can always use a Fateweaver and adjust/redistribute your points so that the
trainer can be used. Basic is ranks 0-3, Advanced is 4-6, and Master is 7-9.

  Basic Training costs roughly 15,000 gold, Advanced Training costs roughly
30,000 gold, and Master Training costs roughly 60,000 gold. When trying to
maximize your stats be sure to use both basic trainers before reading a skill
book or else your +2 starting skill will only be able to receive training from
three of the four trainers.
}}}

                       |           Crafting             |             [17.00.00]
=======================|                                |=======================
                       |________________________________|            
                        ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
{{{
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
                                    Alchemy                           [17.01.00]
________________________________________________________________________________

{{{
  Alchemy allows you to craft various potions that can aid you in your endeavors
throughout Amalur. Each point you invest increases your chances of receiving
reagents when you attempt to harvest them. Certain Milestones let you create new
potions but investing to the maximum level isn't recommended.

Level 1 Milestone - A failed experiment now results in an Unstable Potion.
Level 3 Milestone - You can craft potions with three reagents.
Level 5 Milestone - You can craft potions with four reagents.
Level 10 Milestone - All alchemic recipes discovered.

  Achieving the level five Milestone is the minimum requirement for making
Master level potions but you may want to invest more points into Alchemy so you
harvest reagents more often.

}}}

                                 Blacksmithing                        [17.02.00]
________________________________________________________________________________

{{{
  Blacksmithing lets you salvage parts from weapons and armor, then turn around
and make your own awesome weapons and armor. When Blacksmithing you always
choose a core component that effects the base damage of a weapon or base armor
on defensive items. From least effective to most effective (in level increments
of 0,10,20,30,40):

    Hides - Leather, Boiled Leather, Studded Leather, Trollhide, Dreadscale
    Cloth - Cotton, Linen, Silk, Hexweave, Spiritweave
    Metal - Iron, Steel, Azurite, Sylvanite, Prismere
    Wood  - Birch, Elm, Oak, Ashe, Ebony

  The charts below detail which components go into crafting an item. Note that
chest pieces are the only ones that can be crafted with an Epic Gem.
 ______________________________________________________________________________

                                 Sagecrafting                         [17.03.00]
________________________________________________________________________________

{{{
  Sagecrafting is the art of crafting gems and socketing, or removing, them
into your equipment to improve them. Different levels of Sagecraft let you
craft different levels of gems and all levels increase your chance to
successfully harvest reagents. The creations below are made using Pristine
Shards, but lesser shards still generate the same result just with a lower
value.

  There are other gems that can be created with the same effects but the ones
listed below have the highest values. Example; Lightning + Lightning can yield a
Gem of Sparks but it only does 17 Lightning Damage and 8 Damage over 7 seconds
whilst the Gem of Tempest does 30 and 15 over time.

 ______________________________________________________________________________
|¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ ¯ |
|                                 Weapon Gems                                  |
|_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ |
|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|
| Gem of Incineration                  | Gem of Winter                         |
| - 30 Fire Damage                     | - 30 Ice Damage                       |
| - 20 Burning Damage over 7 seconds   | - 18 Freezing Damage over 6 seconds   |
|                                      |                                       |
| Fire + Magic                         | Ice + Magic                           |
|======================================|=======================================|
| Gem of Tempest                       | Gem of Rot                            |
| - 30 Lightning Damage                | - 48 Poison Damage over 7 seconds     |
| - 15 Shocking Damage over 10 seconds |                                       |
|                                      |                                       |
| Lightning + Magic                    | Poison + Physical                     |
|======================================|=======================================|
| Gem of Slaughter                     | Saboteur's Gem                        |
| - 20 Bleeding Damage over 5 seconds  | - 25 Piercing Damage                  |
